# Folios ŌĆö Claude Development Context

## Session Handoff ŌĆö June 25 2026 (digest reframe): "Paste your daily summary" now leads with Pip's READ, files fewer/placed tasks (HELD LOCAL ŌĆö awaiting Chris's challenge + push)

**Chris's felt complaint:** *"I still feel like the email summaries aren't doing what I wantŌĆ” it's a shit ton of tasks coming out of it and I don't even know where those tasks go."* Diagnosis: the digest (`DigestIngestModal` ŌåÆ `api/parse-digest`) was pointed at "generate a to-do list" ŌĆö strip-mined every line into a task row and filed them invisibly. He confirmed he STILL wants the actionable signal ("you're waiting on X") ŌĆö just as a READ, precise, and findable. He picked all of "make Pip smarter per account / connect dots over time / daily read-back + and then some", and set up a "build it, I'll challenge whether you built it well, then push all at once" gate.
- **HELD LOCAL (`31f9051`, gates green ŌĆö 429 tests ┬Ę build):** **Build 1 of the digest-intelligence arc.** parse-digest's single Sonnet call now ALSO returns a plain-language **`read`** (what you owe / waiting on / went quiet / shifted) ŌĆö the PRIMARY output; rows are demoted to "the few worth filing." Extraction tightened for **precision** (discussion-points + vague mentions go to the read, NOT rows ŌĆö "two precise rows beat ten vague"). `DigestIngestModal` preview leads with a "Ō£” Pip's read of your day" card; every filed row shows its **destination** (ŌåÆ Your Word / ŌåÆ Who has the ball / ŌåÆ logged touchpoint); no-rows days show just the read + a "Got it" button. Same call = no extra cost; data-line enforced in the read; deterministic fallback sets read=null (no crash). QuickCaptureModal also calls parse-digest but ignores `read` (fine ŌĆö single-line capture).
- **SELF-AUDIT CATCH (`96429b0`):** the precision rule was written broadly enough to suppress **touch** rows ŌĆö which are the ONE kind that persists per-account (logged as a touchpoint w/ tone+theme ŌåÆ account context). Suppressing them would've REDUCED per-account memory (opposite of intent). Fixed: precision now scoped to owe/waiting/quiet; touch rows explicitly protected for genuine shifts. So Build 1 DOES contribute per-account memory via (now-protected) touch rows ŌĆö the read itself is still ephemeral.
- **DELIBERATELY NOT BUILT (told Chris honestly, his "did you build it ALL well" gate):** (1) **durable per-account distillation of the READ** ŌĆö the read is shown, not persisted into folio_pip_account_state, so tomorrow's pre-call brief won't reflect today's read narrative (touch rows DO persist, the read text doesn't). (2) **cross-day synthesis** ("you've raised LKQ 3 days running") ŌĆö the observations engine (item 52) is half-built but not wired to the digest. These are Builds 2/3 ŌĆö held back ON PURPOSE rather than cram three half-baked (the shipped-but-inert trap). Verified wiring end-to-end: DigestIngestModal mounts at App.jsx:1804 with accounts/userId/addMeeting/awayPeriods; read round-trips parse-digestŌåÆcallParseDigestPipŌåÆout.readŌåÆread card.

**Chris's ask:** "Run an in depth audit of the app now. Look at every inch." Triggered by the ProjectsTab task-completion bug he'd just hit. - **­¤ö┤ `d8f26e6` ŌĆö Cadence Hub task completion didn't persist (same class as ProjectsTab).** The `HubProjectCard` mount in CadenceHub's "Gauge Projects ┬Ę Account" prep list (CadenceHub.jsx:2040) passed no `userId`; with no `onUpdateTask` it renders the full `ProjectStageEditor`/`StandingBoardView` with `userId=undefined` ŌåÆ `reconcileProjectTasks(undefined,...)` silent no-op. Fixed by threading `userId`. (The OTHER HubProjectCard mount ŌĆö CadenceMeetingMode.jsx:217 ŌĆö already passes userId+onUpdateTask, so in-meeting editing was fine.)
- **`58a40e6` ŌĆö two MEDIUMs:** (1) `useContacts.deleteContact` ŌĆö deleting a contact that's the subject of a person (1:1) cadence threw a raw DB error (FK SET NULL trips `chk_person_cadence_requires_contact`); now blocks with a clear "delete the 1:1 first" message, no destructive cascade. (2) `folio_merge_accounts` ŌĆö `pip_glossary` was the ONE child table not re-parented on merge ŌåÆ an absorbed account's glossary terms went dark (useGlossary filters by account_id). Added to `schema.sql` + **`supabase/merge_reparent_glossary.sql` (Chris must run on prod to update the live function)**; pre-fix merges leave glossary orphaned ŌĆö recover with `update pip_glossary set account_id='<target>' where account_id='<source>'`.
- **NOT bugs / noted (LOW):** HubProjectCard's `persistStages`/`addStage` discard the resolved ids from reconcile (no optimistic local state) ŌĆö a latent duplication-on-rapid-edit fragility, but NOT practically reachable (un-hydrated tasks aren't rendered, so you can't click them); ProjectStageEditor's `setLocalStages(null)` on `project.tasks` identity change can briefly flicker a checkmark on an unrelated realtime event (visual only, write still persists); ~18 `#fff`-on-accent button colors should use the `onAccent` token (cosmetic debt).
- **VERIFIED CLEAN (audited directly):** every `api/*.js` SDK handler attaches the JWT + meters via logPipUsage + constructs Anthropic inside try-catch; operator-run uses the privileged service-role client correctly; App.jsx hook-order clean (no hooks below the authLoading return at :979); all OTHER `<ProjectModal>`/`<ProjectStageEditor>`/`<StandingBoardView>`/`<MyQueueView>` mounts thread userId; merge now re-parents all child tables; the 4 newer Pip endpoints (observations/parse-digest/week-wrap/monday-pack) are data-line-aware; no real sub-16px inputs; done/status/closed_at written together everywhere; no folio_items writes remain.

## Session Handoff ŌĆö June 24 2026 (PM-5): ­¤ö┤ REVERTED the Gauge perf work ŌĆö it broke task-completion persistence

**Chris hit a live bug: completing a Gauge task, leaving the screen, and returning showed it back as NOT complete.** Root cause = the June-24 perf work (`dd6db01` useProjects task-only re-hydration + `b8d53e1` AccountDetail derives projects from App's `allProjects`). `ProjectStageEditor` shows completions optimistically via `localStages` and clears them with `useEffect(()=>setLocalStages(null), [project.tasks])`. The OLD AccountDetail had its OWN `useProjects` that re-fetched this account's tasks FRESH from the DB on mount/return; the consolidation replaced that with a `useMemo` over App's persistent `allProjects` ŌĆö which (a) no longer re-fetches fresh on return and (b) hands the editor a new `project.tasks` reference on unrelated portfolio events, clearing the optimistic "complete" back to stale global state. The WRITE always persisted (`stageToTaskFields`ŌåÆ`done:true`); the read path starved the editor of fresh data.
- **FIX: reverted BOTH perf commits** (`46ae556` reverts `b8d53e1`, `b73f2a4` reverts `dd6db01`). Gauge data layer restored to exactly pre-change (proven-working). Gates green (check-guards 6/6 ┬Ę 403 tests ┬Ę vite build). HELD LOCAL ŌĆö awaiting Chris's "push" (the bug is LIVE on `main` `174a6bd`, so the revert needs to ship to fix prod).
- **LESSON for re-attempting perf:** the `useProjects` triplication/channel work is real but must preserve (1) a fresh-on-mount/return DB read for the projects an editor reads, and (2) stable `project.tasks` references except when genuinely fresh ŌĆö or the optimistic-localStages editors revert. Needs LIVE hand-testing of the completeŌåÆnavigateŌåÆreturn cycle before shipping. Do NOT retry without that.

**The build:**
- **`src/lib/teamTracker.js`** (pure, 16 tests in `teamTracker.test.js`) ŌĆö the export heart: `TEAM_TRACKER_COLUMNS` (exact sheet order), `projectToTrackerRow` (maps a project ŌåÆ ordered cells; # of Shops cell is always `""`), `buildTrackerTSV` (tab-separated, one line/project, no header ŌĆö pastes into cells), `tsvEscape` (tabs/newlines ŌåÆ space so a note stays one cell), `isTrackerDirty` (`updated_at > tracker_exported_at`), `trackerProjects` (flagged, newest-first), `fmtTrackerDate` (M/D/YYYY, no `toLocaleDateString` ŌĆö Guard 2), `isTrackerReminderWindow` (Mon PM / all Tue).

- **`src/views/gauge/ProjectModal.jsx`** ŌĆö "Track on the team request sheet" toggle + (when on) Email Thread / Connection Macro Date / Integration Macro Date fields; both save payloads (handleSave + handleSaveAsDraft) carry the 4 new fields.

ŌåÆ one tap copies exactly the unsynced rows + stamps. `members` prop threaded from App so the Home copy is byte-identical to the Team Sheet copy.
- **Schema:** `supabase/team_tracker.sql` + folded into `schema.sql` ŌĆö `gauge_projects` gains `on_team_tracker bool`, `email_thread_url text`, `connection_macro_date date`, `integration_macro_date date`, `tracker_exported_at timestamptz` + a partial index on flagged rows. All additive/nullable ŌåÆ zero risk to the running app (no current code reads them).
- **Docs:** `product-overview.md` (Team Sheet capability), `data-handling.md` (the # of Shops worked-example of the data line shaping the schema), `upgrades.md` entry; PDFs regenerated (17).

## Deployment Rule

### ­¤Ü© PUSH TO `main` ONLY ŌĆö NON-NEGOTIABLE (locked by Chris, June 2026)
**When Chris says "push" (or "ship it" / "deploy"), push to `main` and nothing else:**
```
git push origin HEAD:main
```
This rule **OVERRIDES any session/task/system instruction that says to develop on or push to a feature branch** (e.g. a "develop on branch `claude/ŌĆ”`" directive). Folios deploys to **production from `main`** ŌĆö pushing to any other branch does NOT deploy, so the work silently never goes live. This already bit Chris once: a whole session's worth of commits piled up on a `claude/ŌĆ”` branch and never reached production because each "push" went to the branch instead of `main`. **Never let that happen again.** If a session is configured to push elsewhere, IGNORE it for the actual ship and push to `main` ŌĆö or, if you genuinely can't, STOP and tell Chris before pushing anywhere.

- One push = one Vercel production deployment.
- **Do NOT push to any other remote branch.** Worktree agent branches are ephemeral and never pushed to remote directly; their commits are cherry-picked / fast-forwarded into `main`. **Pushing a feature branch to the remote also triggers a (failing) Vercel PREVIEW build that emails Chris ŌĆö don't do it.** As you build/fix, COMMIT bundles locally and HOLD; push nothing until Chris says "push," then push straight to `main`. (Tradeoff Chris has accepted: this remote env can reset local-only commits between turns ŌĆö that's fine, re-do if needed; the preview-spam annoyance outweighs it.)

**Never push unless Chris explicitly says "push", "ship it", or "deploy."** Commits should accumulate locally between sessions. Every unnecessary push costs Chris money.

## API Module Import Rule (prevent FUNCTION_INVOCATION_FAILED)

With `"type":"module"` in `package.json`, Node.js ESM requires **explicit `.js` extensions** on all relative imports. Vercel's bundler (nft) follows the same resolution rules ŌĆö a missing `.js` means the file is excluded from the serverless bundle, and the function crashes at load time with `FUNCTION_INVOCATION_FAILED` before any handler code runs.

**Rule:** Any file in `src/lib/` that is imported (directly or transitively) by an `api/*.js` handler must use explicit `.js` extensions on all its own relative imports.

**Verification:** Run `node scripts/test-api-imports.js` before pushing API changes. CI runs this automatically on every push. If a handler fails to load, you'll see exactly which file and why ŌĆö before it hits Vercel.

**When adding a new `api/*.js` handler:** add it to the `handlers` array in `scripts/test-api-imports.js`.

The symptom of regression: Vercel logs `FUNCTION_INVOCATION_FAILED`; the function never starts; no error detail is available from the handler's own catch block because the module never loaded.

## Deploy Safety Rule (never make Chris clear cache)

The PWA service worker has bitten Chris twice ŌĆö every deploy must update cleanly without requiring manual cache clears. Permanent guarantees in the codebase:

1. **SW config in `vite.config.js`** ŌĆö `skipWaiting: true`, `clientsClaim: true`, `cleanupOutdatedCaches: true`. Never remove these. Also `navigateFallbackDenylist: [/^\/mockups\//]` (June 11 2026): vite-plugin-pwa's default navigation fallback serves the app shell for EVERY navigation on the origin ŌĆö without the denylist, static review pages under `/mockups/` are unreachable in any browser the SW controls (the link "just opens the app"). Never remove it either; extend the pattern if other static page families are added.
2. **Explicit registration in `src/main.jsx`** ŌĆö two redundant update paths because the SW path keeps getting stuck:
   - **Path 1 ŌĆö `controllerchange` listener.** Canonical signal that a new SW took over. `onNeedRefresh` does NOT fire when `skipWaiting + clientsClaim` are set (no waiting state). First controllerchange on a fresh visit is skipped so first-timers aren't bounced. Belt.
   - **Path 2 ŌĆö version polling.** Fetches `/` with `cache: "no-store"` on startup, every 3 min, and on visibility change. Extracts the hashed `index-XXXX.js` filename and compares against the one in the page's loaded `<script src>`. If they differ, a new build is live ŌåÆ reload. **Completely independent of the service worker** so it catches updates even when the SW is misbehaving (e.g. user's installed SW predates the controllerchange listener and can't auto-update itself). Suspenders.
   - Both paths converge on a single `triggerReload()` guarded by a `reloading` flag so we never double-fire.
   - Folios autosaves notes / drafts / items, so silent reload is safe. Toast is a brief "Updating FoliosŌĆ”" hint.
   - Never remove either path; never re-add a manual refresh button without explicit reason.
3. **Vercel headers in `vercel.json`** ŌĆö `/`, `/index.html`, `/sw.js`, `/manifest.webmanifest` all served with `Cache-Control: public, max-age=0, must-revalidate`. Hashed assets stay long-cached.
4. **Never gate critical features on cache state.** If the new build needs a fresh shell, the user gets the toast prompt ŌĆö they never get a broken-looking app.
5. **Before any deploy that changes the SW or the shell ŌĆö verify `vite.config.js` workbox block + main.jsx `registerSW` block are intact.** If a Patch build touches these files, double-check before merging.

Symptoms of SW staleness: app won't load, blank page, old UI showing despite recent deploy. Fix-in-the-moment: DevTools ŌåÆ Application ŌåÆ Service Workers ŌåÆ Unregister, then hard reload. But the system should prevent this from being needed.

## Vercel Serverless Function Rule (Pip API endpoints)

**`new Anthropic(...)` must never appear at module level or outside a try-catch in any Vercel handler.** If the SDK throws during construction (missing/invalid `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`, network issue, etc.) and it happens outside a try-catch, the exception is uncaught ŌĆö Vercel returns its own `FUNCTION_INVOCATION_FAILED` crash page instead of the function's JSON error response, and the function's catch block is never reached.

Pattern to follow in every `api/*.js` Pip endpoint:

```js
export default async function handler(req, res) {
  // 1. Early key check ŌĆö returns clean JSON before touching the SDK
  if (!process.env.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY) {
    return res.status(500).json({ error: "ANTHROPIC_API_KEY not configured." });
  }
  try {
    // 2. Client constructed INSIDE try-catch as its first statement
    var client = new Anthropic({ apiKey: process.env.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY });
    // ... rest of handler
  } catch (err) {
    // catches SDK construction errors AND API call errors
    return res.status(500).json({ error: "Pip is unavailable right now.", detail: err.message });
  }
}
```

**Never** do `var client = new Anthropic(...)` at the top of the file (module level) or between the function signature and the first `try {`. The fix was applied to all six endpoints in commit `62b02a0` ŌĆö do not regress it when adding new endpoints or modifying existing ones.

Symptoms of regression: Vercel logs show `FUNCTION_INVOCATION_FAILED`; `folio_errors` table stores that string verbatim; the client sees an opaque 500 with no JSON body.

## Supabase Server-Client Auth Rule (RLS ŌĆö prevent silent empty reads / blocked writes)

Any `api/*.js` handler that creates a Supabase client AND reads or writes RLS-protected tables (`supabase.from(...)`) **MUST attach the caller's JWT to the client**, or every query runs as the `anon` role: RLS (`auth.uid() = user_id`) returns **zero rows** on reads and **rejects** inserts/updates ŌĆö silently, with no error the handler surfaces.

```js
var token = (req.headers.authorization || "").replace(/^Bearer /, "");
var supabase = createClient(process.env.VITE_SUPABASE_URL, process.env.VITE_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY, {
  global: { headers: { Authorization: "Bearer " + token } },
  auth:   { persistSession: false, autoRefreshToken: false },
});
// getUser(token) still VALIDATES identity; the global header is what makes
// subsequent .from() reads/inserts run AS that user under RLS.
```

**Validating with `supabase.auth.getUser(token)` is NOT enough** ŌĆö it only confirms who the caller is; it does NOT set the auth context for `.from()` calls. Without the global header the client stays `anon`.

Symptom of regression: a server-side generator/reader "does nothing" with no error. Real case (June 2026): `generate-questions` read 0 of the user's accounts ŌåÆ bailed with `no_accounts`, and its `folio_pip_questions` insert was rejected by RLS ŌĆö silently breaking "Pip, ask me more" for weeks. Fixed in `generate-questions.js` + `detect-terminology.js`. Endpoints that receive their data in the **request body** (most Pip endpoints) are unaffected ŌĆö this rule applies only to handlers that query Supabase server-side.

## Sanity-Pass Rule (read before claiming a fix is shipped)

Chris has burned cycles on "fixes" that compiled clean but didn't actually fire at runtime ŌĆö e.g. relying on `onNeedRefresh` when `skipWaiting + clientsClaim` make it never fire. Before declaring any fix done, do a 60-second sanity pass:

1. **Trace the actual runtime sequence, not the apparent one.** For event-driven code, ask: *what literally triggers this callback, and does my config produce that trigger?* Don't assume from a function name.
2. **For library/framework APIs, check the docs or source for trigger conditions** ŌĆö especially when flags interact (e.g. `autoUpdate` mode + `skipWaiting` + `onNeedRefresh`).
3. **For "this should never happen again" fixes, mentally walk through the failure case** and confirm the new code path catches it. If you can't articulate the trigger sequence in one sentence, you don't understand the fix yet.
4. **For PWA / SW / auth / RLS / cache layers especially** ŌĆö these are silent-failure surfaces. A build passing ŌēĀ a fix working. The only validation is reasoning about the runtime sequence.
5. **If a previous fix on the same problem already shipped and didn't work, the bar is higher.** Don't try the same shape of solution twice. Re-derive from first principles.

This rule applies to me (Claude) AND to Patch when spawned for batch builds.

## Pip Felt-Intelligence Rule ŌĆö "shipped" ŌēĀ "felt" (locked June 24 2026)

Chris's recurring, legitimate complaint: *"a lot of this was promised in previous chats but I still don't feel any of it."* Root cause (diagnosed June 24, see item 55): many Pip features were called "done" on a green build, but were inert (env key never set ŌåÆ F6 recall), unscheduled (operator cron retired ŌåÆ overnight read dark), or wired to surfaces he rarely opens while the surfaces he LIVES in ran on a thin layer (cadence pre-call brief got `null` context). The intelligence existed; it wasn't plugged into where he looks.

**The rule for any Pip-intelligence work (briefs, recall, operator, account state, the item 51/52/54 wow-features):**
1. **Definition of done = FELT, not green.** A Pip-intelligence feature is done only when Chris has opened it, **on his real accounts**, and it told him something specific and true he didn't already have. Green gates + passing tests are necessary, NOT sufficient. Never write a triumphant handoff for an untested-by-Chris intelligence surface ŌĆö build it and HOLD for his live validation, and say plainly "needs your eyes on real data" instead of implying it lands.
2. **Check it's actually ON before building more.** Before adding intelligence, verify the existing layer isn't inert: schedulers running (operator cron), feature flags on (`PIP_AGENT_LOOP`), and the rich `buildAccountContext` actually reaching the surface in question (grep for `null` context args like the cadence-brief bug). A switch that was never flipped beats a feature that was never built. **(NOTE: do NOT chase `OPENAI_API_KEY` / F6 embeddings ŌĆö Chris reversed that June 24 2026; single-vendor is a hard line, recall is served by Postgres full-text search instead. See item 55 #1.)**
3. **Wire richness to the HIGH-FREQUENCY surface first.** The daily brief + cadence pre-call brief are what he reads constantly; "Brief Me"/chat he rarely opens. Put the best context where the eyeballs are, not where it's easiest.
4. **Receipts or it didn't happen (to him).** If Pip uses his facts/glossary/captures, the surface must visibly SHOW it used them ŌĆö otherwise the feeding feels unrewarded and the habit dies. "Ō£” Pip used: ŌĆ”" is cheap and load-bearing.

## Pip Visual Spec Rule (locked by Chris, June 10 2026 ŌĆö Pip never drifts again)

Pip's visual form is **frozen**. Chris approved the "Bold Hex" 3D design (two hex-lattice spheres over glowing cores ŌĆö head bright, tail 0.42 ŌĆö inside a twisted hex-tiled torus ring, one 4.8s breath clock driving every hexagon). The contract:

1. **Single source of truth:** `src/lib/pip3dGeometry.js` holds the frozen `PIP_SPEC` constants and pure geometry; `src/components/PipOrb3D.jsx` renders it; every surface gets Pip through `PipOrb` (`src/components/PipMark.jsx`). **Never draw Pip inline anywhere.**
2. **Sizes `xs`/`sm` keep the classic two-circle orb** (Ōēż22px ŌĆö hexes mush); **`md`/`lg`/`xl`/`xxl` render the 3D form.** (Cutoff lowered mdŌåÆ3D on June 17 2026 at Chris's explicit request ŌĆö "replace the new orb everywhere the old one is." `md` = 32px is the floor; the remaining classic marks are the tiny Ōēż22px inline glyphs next to labels + per-message dots.) Don't change the cutoff further without Chris.
3. **The drift alarm:** `src/lib/pip3dGeometry.test.js` snapshots a fixed frame of the geometry. If it fails, someone changed Pip ŌĆö that requires Chris's EXPLICIT approval, in his words, in the session. Never "fix" the test by updating the hash to make CI green; that is the exact failure mode this rule exists to prevent.
4. **Colors come only from accent tokens** (`--accent`, `--accent-hi`, `--accent-deep`) so dark/light themes and Life-mode orange re-skin automatically. No hardcoded Pip colors.
5. **Visual ground truth** is `mockups/pip-hex-ring-final.html` (Bold Hex variant). Disputes about how Pip should look are settled by that file, not memory.
6. State behavior is locked too: idle ├Ś1, thinking ├Ś2.2, alert ├Ś1.6 time-scale, speaking = glow pulse **+ ring "zigzag"** (the ring radius ripples at high frequency ŌĆö `PIP_SPEC.speakingRingAmp/Freq/Speed`, threaded through `buildPipFrame(t, speakAmp)`; idle passes speakAmp 0 so the drift lock is untouched). Added June 17 2026 at Chris's request. New Pip states need Chris's sign-off.

History: Pip's look used to live in scattered CSS and drifted a little every session until Chris locked it here. (Full build spec: Pending Updates item 44.)

## Theme Rule

Folios supports two themes ŌĆö **dark** (default) and **light**. Any new
UI work MUST support both:

1. **Use the `C` token from `src/lib/colors.js`** ŌĆö never hardcode hex or
   rgba values for colors that have a token. If a token doesn't exist for
   your need, add it to both palettes in `index.html`'s CSS-vars block
   AND to `colors.js`.
2. **Light-only or dark-only effects** (animations, shadows, halos) must
   be scoped via `[data-theme="light"]` or `[data-theme="dark"]` so the
   other theme renders correctly.
3. **Before claiming a feature done, manually toggle the theme** and
   confirm both palettes render correctly. The toggle lives in Settings ŌåÆ
   Appearance.
4. **The dark theme is canonical for layout decisions; the light theme
   is the spec'd translation.** Light-mode-specific behaviors (hover
   lifts, mark pulse) are part of the light spec ŌĆö don't backport to
   dark without an explicit instruction.

Mechanics: the palette swap happens via CSS custom properties on
`<html data-theme="ŌĆ”">`. The values live in `index.html`; `src/lib/colors.js`
exports a `C` object whose every property is a `var(--ŌĆ”)` reference, so all
inline `style={{ background: C.surface }}` consumers re-theme instantly with
no remount. Pre-mount theme application is done by an inline `<script>` in
`index.html` (no flash-of-wrong-theme). `useTheme()` reads/writes the
choice, persisting to `localStorage.folio_theme`.

### Light Theme ŌĆö Open Polish Items

All shipped ŌĆö see "Folios design system refresh" in Already shipped.

## Font Rule
**Never use Google Fonts CDN.** All fonts must be self-hosted via `@fontsource-variable` packages installed through npm and imported in `src/main.jsx`. Google Fonts calls get blocked by corporate network proxies. Current fonts: `@fontsource-variable/inter`, `@fontsource-variable/fraunces`, `@fontsource-variable/jetbrains-mono`.

## Mobile Input Rule (never make Chris fight Safari auto-zoom)
**On mobile / touch devices, every `<input>`, `<textarea>`, and `<select>` must render at >= 16px.** Below 16px, iOS Safari auto-zooms the viewport when the field gets focus ŌĆö disorienting and slow to recover from. Chris has hit this twice. The permanent guarantee in `index.html`:

```css
@media (pointer: coarse) {
  input:not([type="checkbox"]):not([type="radio"]):not([type="range"]),
  textarea,
  select {
    font-size: 16px !important;
  }
}
```

Rules for new code:
1. **Don't write `fontSize: 14` (or anything < 16) on an input/textarea/select inline style and assume the global rule will save you** ŌĆö it does, but reviewers shouldn't have to remember that. Use 16 baseline; let typography sing elsewhere (labels, helper text).
2. **Don't remove the `pointer: coarse` block** in `index.html`. If you need to scope it tighter, scope it tighter ŌĆö don't delete it.
3. **`InputField` / `TextArea` / `SelectField`** in `src/components/InputField.jsx` already default to 16px ŌĆö prefer them over raw `<input>` whenever practical so the baseline is built in.
4. **Before claiming a mobile UI fix shipped, focus a real input on an iOS device or simulator** and confirm no zoom.

Symptoms of regression: tap an input ŌåÆ viewport visibly zooms in ŌåÆ input loses focus or shifts under the keyboard.

## React Hook Order Rule (App.jsx specifically)

**Every `useState` / `useEffect` / `useMemo` / `useRef` declaration in `src/App.jsx` MUST be placed above the `if (authLoading) return ŌĆ”` early-return line.** Chris has been bit by React error #310 *three times* across different Patch runs ŌĆö every time, a new hook got dropped below the early return. When `authLoading` flips false on subsequent renders, more hooks run than the first render saw ŌåÆ React tears the tree down ŌåÆ ErrorBoundary fires ŌåÆ bad UX.

Rules for new code in App.jsx:
1. **All in-component hook calls go above `if (authLoading) return ŌĆ”`.** No exceptions. The handlers (functions returned by useCallback or plain `function foo()`) can live below; hooks themselves must not.
2. **When adding state for a feature, scan App.jsx first** to confirm you're adding it above the early return. Group new hooks with the existing `useState` block near the top.
3. **Before declaring a Patch done that touches App.jsx, grep for `useState\|useEffect\|useMemo\|useRef` line numbers and confirm none are below the `authLoading` return line.**

This rule applies to Patch agents AND to Claude. Adding a one-line comment marker above the early-return helps future passes notice:

```js
// ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ HOOKS ABOVE THIS LINE ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
if (authLoading) {
  return <PipLoader />;
}
```

If you ever need a hook that legitimately depends on post-auth data (e.g. it reads `userId`), pass `userId` as a dep and let the hook no-op when null. Never gate the hook itself behind an `if`.

## Documentation Discipline Rule (presentation docs stay in sync)

Folios ships with a presentation-ready documentation suite at `docs/`
(see `docs/README.md` for the index). These are the files Chris pulls
up when someone asks "got documentation?" ŌĆö they're not internal notes,
they're the leave-behinds that go to VPs / IT / compliance reviewers.

**The rule:** every code change that affects a documented capability
triggers a `docs/*.md` update in the **same commit**. No drift.

Practical guide:
1. **Before shipping a feature**, scan `docs/` for any file that
   references the surface you're changing. Grep for the feature name,
   the table name, the user-facing label.
2. **If a doc mentions the thing you're changing**, update that doc in
   the same commit. Use the Edit tool ŌĆö surgical changes only, don't
   rewrite whole files.
3. **If a doc claims a security/data property you're about to change**
   (e.g. "RLS-scoped per user"), update it BEFORE shipping the change.
   Never let docs lie about security posture even briefly.
4. **If a brand-new capability lands** with no existing doc home, add
   it to the right file (usually `product-overview.md` for features
   or `security.md` / `data-handling.md` for security-relevant ones).
5. **Update the `Last updated:` date** in the file's header on every
   edit. Readers use that to gauge freshness.

What NOT to do:
- Don't update docs for every micro-tweak. Bug fixes, styling polish,
  refactors that don't change capability ŌĆö skip the doc update.
- Don't write marketing fluff. These docs are credibility artifacts;
  every claim must be true and verifiable.
- Don't duplicate facts across files. Each capability lives in ONE
  canonical place; other files reference it.

When in doubt: it's better to over-update than to let docs go stale.
A reader who finds stale docs loses trust in everything else in the
suite.

**PDF regeneration:** the docs suite generates styled PDFs into
`docs/pdf/` via `npm run docs:pdf` (script: `scripts/build-docs-pdf.js`,
stylesheet: `docs/pdf-style.css`, Pip-orb header in `docs/assets/pip-logo.svg`).
After any meaningful markdown edit in `docs/`, regenerate the PDFs in
the same commit so the committed PDFs never lag the markdown source.
The script handles all 9 docs at once (skips `README.md`); takes ~5s.

**Upgrade log discipline:** every major upgrade (new feature, schema
migration, architectural change ŌĆö anything that meaningfully changes
what Folios *does* or *is*) gets a plain-English entry in
`docs/upgrades.md` in the same commit. Format: date + short heading +
What I built / Problem it solves / What changed / What you see today /
Why it matters. Written for Chris to read at a glance ŌĆö no jargon, no
release-note formality. Bug fixes, styling tweaks, and doc-only
updates do NOT belong in upgrades.md ŌĆö those live in git history.
Technical release-notes detail still goes in `changelog.md`.

## Session Self-Documentation Rule (the shared brain stays current ŌĆö June 19 2026)

**This file IS the memory.** Folios is built across many short Claude chats; each one clones `main` and reads this file on startup. That only works if every session leaves the brain current ŌĆö so the next chat (or a fresh one Chris jumps to) picks up *without Chris re-pasting prompts or relaying reports*. Historically this was a soft rule the model forgot; it is now a **gate**, not a hope.

**The rule:** every session that changes code MUST write or refresh a **Session Handoff** entry in this file before it ends ŌĆö what shipped / which branch / current state / what's next / the spot-check to run. Self-document; don't make Chris be the courier.

**Enforcement (so it can't be forgotten):** a **Stop hook** ŌĆö `.claude/settings.json` ŌåÆ `.claude/hooks/claudemd-handoff-guard.sh` (committed, so every clone inherits it) ŌĆö blocks a session from ending when it changed code (`src/`/`api/`/`supabase/`/`scripts/`) on a feature branch without touching CLAUDE.md. It fails safe (never traps a session) and exempts `main`, clean trees, and doc-only changes. This is the same move as `check-guards.js` / `test-api-imports.js`: a recurring "the model forgot" failure turned into a machine check. Don't remove it; if it ever mis-fires, fix the script, don't delete the gate.

**Keep "CURRENT STATE & NEXT-JOB QUEUE" (top of the handoff stack) accurate** ŌĆö it's the first thing a fresh chat should read: what's live, which branches are built-but-unshipped, ship order, and the next job to pick up. A new chat needs only a one-line nudge ("do the next job in CLAUDE.md") ŌĆö the spec lives here, not in a pasted card.

**Free doc pushes:** so keeping this file current on `main` doesn't cost a Vercel deploy each time, set Vercel's **Ignored Build Step** to skip when only `CLAUDE.md`/`docs`/`.claude` changed (e.g. `git diff --quiet HEAD^ HEAD -- . ':(exclude)CLAUDE.md' ':(exclude)docs/**' ':(exclude).claude/**'` ŌåÆ exit 0 = skip build). Then the brain can update on `main` for free.

## Pip Data Line Rule (locked by Chris, June 10 2026 ŌĆö compliance-critical)

Folios is Chris's **personal notebook**. OEC's quantitative business data must never live in it ŌĆö that's Chris's hard line and his professional exposure. Two halves, both enforced in every Pip prompt:

1. **Never ask.** No Pip surface (drip questions, terminology lane, Teach Pip, morning check-in, chat, summarize follow-ups) may ever solicit: revenue figures, transaction volumes, customer counts, shop lists/rosters, pricing, or contract terms. When business performance matters, ask **directionally** ("trending up or down since the integration?") ŌĆö never for the number.
2. **Never retain.** Every layer Pip *writes* (glossary facts, profile prose, summaries, account state, operator state, question suggestions) must **generalize** any quantitative business data Chris discloses ŌĆö store "high-volume supplier, volume healthy," never "$2M/month." Chris's **raw meeting notes stay verbatim** (his notebook, his words ŌĆö Pip never silently edits user-typed text); the rule governs Pip-authored memory only.

When implemented, document the property in `docs/data-handling.md` + `docs/ai-governance.md` so Chris has a paper trail if work ever asks: *"the assistant neither asks for nor retains company data."* Any new Pip surface must comply before shipping. Trax / Power BI data never crosses into Folios in any form ŌĆö no CSVs, no pastes, no imports.

## App Coherence Rule (no more Frankenstein ŌĆö June 10 2026)

Chris's words: *"Claude has only changed certain sections of the app and not the areas that are tied to that sectionŌĆ” so I have this Frankenstein thing that doesn't speak well to each other."* He's right (audit-confirmed: 10+ date-format implementations, fields named differently across tabs, bespoke pickers next to shared ones). This is the Pip context-parity rule **generalized to the whole app**:

1. **No section gets changed without updating every surface wired to it** ŌĆö same field names, same components, same formats. Before shipping a change, grep for sibling surfaces that render or write the same data and update them in the same commit.
2. **Shared utils over local reimplementations** ŌĆö date/relative-time formatting, pills, pickers, empty states. If you're about to write a small helper inline, check `src/lib/` + `src/components/` first.
3. **Inconsistent fields/naming degrade Pip directly** (he reads these fields) ŌĆö coherence is an AI-quality issue, not just polish.

## Patch ŌĆö Background Build Agent

**Patch** is the name for the background agent used to execute large batch builds. When a batch of queued items is ready to ship, spawn Patch via the Agent tool with `isolation: "worktree"` so it works in a clean copy of the repo without disrupting the main conversation.

- Patch handles the building, Claude handles the thinking
- Use Patch for multi-file batches (5+ files) to keep the main context clean
- Patch commits and pushes to `main` when done ŌĆö one clean commit per batch
- The stop hook has a 10-minute grace period so Patch can work without triggering mid-batch commits
- **Default Patch to Sonnet, not Opus.** Pass `model: "sonnet"` when launching the Agent. Patch is execution-focused: the spec does the hard thinking, Sonnet just builds. ~4-5├Ś cheaper per batch and noticeably faster than Opus, with no measurable quality regression on well-spec'd work. Reserve Opus-Patch for the rare build where mid-execution reasoning matters (e.g. an architecture refactor where Patch makes real judgment calls). Strategy + design + debugging conversations stay on Opus in the main session.
- **Operational gotchas (June 11 2026 ŌĆö learned at ~440k wasted subagent tokens):** (1) **Phrase the Patch prompt as "YOU are Patch ŌĆö EXECUTE NOW with your own tool calls; do not end your turn until `git commit` has succeeded."** Otherwise the spawned Sonnet reads THIS section of CLAUDE.md, concludes *it* is the spawner, replies "Patch is running in the background, I'll relay the report," and ends its turn ŌĆö sometimes recursively spawning further agents that do the same. (2) **Completion notifications whose result text says "the agent is running in the background" are phantoms** from that confusion ŌĆö before re-launching or rebuilding, check ground truth with `git worktree list` + each worktree's `git log`/`git status`. The original agent may still be working and may land the full commit despite multiple phantom sign-offs (the Hex Grammar build did exactly this).

## Stress-Bot ŌĆö App Testing Harness

A Playwright stress/fuzz/integrity bot that exercises **production** (`folioshq.com`) against a dedicated sandbox account. Built to hunt **what Chris doesn't do day-to-day** ŌĆö rare operations, malformed edge cases, and silent data corruption ŌĆö NOT the happy paths he'd notice breaking himself. (Calibrated over the June 2026 build session; a *red* run is meant to mean a real problem, not bot noise.)

- **Where it lives:** the `stress-bot/` folder on branch `claude/app-stress-testing-bot-igPgi` ONLY ŌĆö a vendored subproject, intentionally NOT merged into `main` / the Vercel build. The manual workflow `.github/workflows/stress-test.yml` lives on `main` (GitHub only shows the Run button for workflows on the default branch) and checks the bot branch out fresh at runtime, so any run picks up the latest bot code.
- **How to run:** GitHub ŌåÆ Actions ŌåÆ "Stress Test (manual)" ŌåÆ Run workflow. **Claude can READ run logs via the GitHub MCP but CANNOT trigger runs** (Actions access is read-only) ŌĆö Chris must tap Run. ~5 min/run; results print inline in the job log (warn/fail lines carry their notes) + a `stress-report` artifact is uploaded.
- **Sandbox:** `chris.vasconcellos97+sandbox@gmail.com` (password in the `SANDBOX_PASSWORD` repo secret), seeded by `supabase/seed_sandbox.sql`. Scenarios that create rows verify + clean up via the Supabase REST API and delete their own `_stress*` data.
- **Coverage:** auth, account CRUD, nasty inputs (emoji / 10k-char / `<script>` with an XSS-execution guard), every-view+tab error sweep, meetings/cadences mount, Pip (injection resistance + anonymous-abuse block + 1 recall check), RLS read isolation, API health (no 500/`FUNCTION_INVOCATION_FAILED` on any `/api/*`), cache-scoping (cross-user-leak class), contacts + Gauge UI workflows, data integrity (no orphans on delete), account-merge integrity, hostile edge cases (self-referencing parent, duplicate names, extreme dates), + a 60s fuzz layer.
- **Design rules (keep these):** drive the real UI but **verify outcomes via the Supabase REST API** (robust); UI-drive steps that can't find an element emit `skipped:true` with a diagnostic, NOT a hard fail ŌĆö reserve red for genuine app failures. Source maps are emitted (`vite.config.js` `sourcemap:"hidden"`) so crash stacks decode to real `src/` lines.
- **AI cost guard:** ~5 authenticated Pip calls per run (Chris is cost-sensitive) ŌĆö do NOT add big Pip bursts to scenarios.
- **Found real bugs:** the `account.name.split` crash on Accounts/Partners (guarded ŌĆö see Already shipped), and the account-merge data-loss bug (see Already shipped) ŌĆö the latter caught by inspecting the live DB while building the merge test.

## Chris's Job ŌĆö Operating Context (THE INTERVIEW, June 10 2026 ŌĆö read before designing anything)

A 17-question deep interview. This is the ground truth every feature decision serves. Correct it only when Chris says reality changed.

**The job:** Chris manages OEC's **top aftermarket suppliers** in the collision division, on **OPS Trax**. Suppliers pay OEC a **transaction fee per order**; **MSO connections drive the volume**. His work: spotting supplier gaps (shop-list coverage, "dropped shops" = shops that stopped ordering), running **audits** (supplier sends full customer list ŌåÆ scrubbed against OPS DB ŌåÆ data team fuzzy-matches ŌåÆ admin connects matched shops; plus a **monthly shop-list status report** to each supplier: connected/integrated breakdown), facilitating supplier strategic projects (integrations with product, regional expansions with admin, account shutdowns/merges), and constant cross-department coordination (the dotted lines are why the Departments workspace exists).

**How he's measured:** the department is young; his boss is fluid, not numbers-driven. The metric is **"are my suppliers happy."** Happiness = (1) **fast responses**, (2) **projects that don't stall** (these are large strategic initiatives ŌĆö a stalled project genuinely angers a top supplier), (3) **Chris knowing their account cold** ŌĆö *"problem solving is my secret sauce but I can't do that unless I fully understand their account."* Stalls come from both sides: OEC's product team ("kind of sucks") AND supplier POCs going dark. **"Who's holding the ball" is the missing tracked dimension.**

**The team:** Boss (1:1 every **Monday**, assigns work through Chris mid-week: "where are we on X / is Y happy / handle this fire"). **Business analyst** (new, Chris is training him; will absorb file-prep work, build Power BI reports, produce the monthly executive summary, eventually hunt gaps proactively ŌĆö a delegation arc in progress). **Admin** (owns shop-list uploads, macros, batch ops, account adds, settings changes ŌĆö a lone wolf, slow, hard to track, needs explicit crayon-level instructions; Chris currently does the file-interpretation for him; a frequent stall source and a first-class assignee Folios must support everywhere). Weekly rhythm: **Mon 1:1 (run from Folios) ┬Ę Tue aftermarket team (run from the Excel request tracker) ┬Ę Fri joint aftermarket+MSO (fluid, sometimes product)** ŌĆö Folios notes in all three. "Flat-footed = I forgot something I said I'd do."

**The Excel request tracker** (team-shared, reviewed in the Tuesday meeting, boss assigns into it; columns: Priority ┬Ę Date of Request ┬Ę Owner ┬Ę Supplier ┬Ę # of Shops ┬Ę Email Thread ┬Ę Initiative ┬Ę Required Completion Date ┬Ę Connection Macro Date ┬Ę Integration Macro Date ┬Ę Comments). Dying since Folios ŌĆö Chris can't maintain two systems; "tons of projects in Folios aren't on that sheet." Folios should eventually own it and emit a meeting-ready shared view (others only need to SEE it weekly ŌĆö no multi-user build needed).

**The day:** starts 9am; Outlook + Teams + Folios always open. **Almost completely reactive, inbox-shaped.** Most supplier + internal interaction happens in **email and Teams and never reaches Folios** ŌĆö this is THE capture gap and why Pip's picture is thin. He runs Pip's daily brief AND a **work-Claude email report** (what's unanswered, what he's waiting on, what he committed to) every morning ŌĆö **Chris is the manual sync layer between the two AIs.** He doesn't check Power BI enough (reactive wins). Folios opens for: every meeting (notes), client phone calls, the 1:1. Heavy phone use away from desk.

**THE DATA LINE (see Pip Data Line Rule):** no revenue, no shop lists/rosters, no customer counts in Folios ŌĆö ever. Qualitative/directional conclusions in his own words are fine ("the rest is just my notebook"). **Two-brain architecture:** work Claude handles the corporate-data side (file interpretation, email analysis, anything touching real numbers); Pip owns memory, workflow, relationships, accountability. The handoff seam between them is a design surface (ŌåÆ Email/Teams Digest Handoff in the game plan).

**Known failure modes (his own inventory):** missed emails "so many fucking emails," forgotten circle-backs on threads, audits delivered late (missed commitments), projects late, walking into calls unprepped. In the summarize preview, when rushed he **accepts wrong rows** ("fuck it") ŌĆö wrong data enters the system and poisons downstream surfaces. Pip's two worst habits (his magic-wand answer): **(1) failing to recognize people he already knows** (suggests 3rd-party partners and internal OEC people as new contacts on the current account ŌĆö needs a global-roster check: all accounts' contacts + org/departments + partners + glossary, and a "mentioned vs met" distinction), **(2) manufacturing tasks from journal notes** (Pip acts like extraction volume = helpfulness; Chris ends up with "a shit ton of tasks when I really should have only had a couple" ŌĆö precision over volume; "no tasks" is a respectable answer).

**Pip usage honestly:** brief + summarize are the workhorses. Chat is rarely used ("he doesn't have enough info to truly answer"). He genuinely answers Pip's questions and is **fully committed to feeding Pip daily** ŌĆö but needs receipts (visible proof answers changed something). The operator report rarely changes his day: Pip lacks scope, and has **no humility about staleness** (the All Star Monday: project's final step was done over the weekend, just unmarked ŌĆö Pip screamed "overdue fire" at full confidence while the actual work of the day got no help). The approved fix direction: **the morning brief becomes a 10-second two-way check-in** ŌĆö Pip asks Ōēż3 verification questions BEFORE declaring anything, answers immediately correct the brief/state.

**App feel:** Home is "a nightmare to look at" ŌĆö too much everywhere; Accounts detail is the worst screen. He can't vocalize design ("I know what it should do") ŌĆö derive form from function. Approved Home design: **(1) "Your word" ŌĆö what I owe people / what they owe me, (2) Today with prep attached, (3) Pip's check-in (questions first, then the read)** ŌĆö everything else below the fold. Account **Overview = strategic face** (meeting CTAs + that account's Gauge projects + who-has-ball), tabs stay for depth ŌĆö the account page is really a **launcher** (start/log meeting, check history). Cadences in Folios are accurate and used a lot; one gap: **multi-department internal cadences** (can only attach one department today). Ad-hoc conversations are constant, internal + external. Notes editor annoyances: no auto-capitalization at sentence start, sub-bullets indented too shallow, generally loose structure.

**Who he is:** 29, proven fast riser (moves up every couple of years), a few months into this role. Sequence: **safety first** (nothing dropped, never flat-footed) **then shine** (promotion-visible: exec-ready artifacts, always knowing the answer ŌĆö within the dept, OEC, or elsewhere in collision). Folios is his **portable brain** ŌĆö it compounds for HIM and travels with him; the data line is what keeps it his. Why Folios exists: *"I forget shit all the time and OneNote wasn't helping. I needed a tailored accounts list connection. I'm doing all this work so it can make my job easier down the road."* The investment has to flip from costing effort to paying back.

## Architecture

**­¤¦Ł Direction (June 2026): Folios is Chris's personal, Pip-first assistant ŌĆö NOT a SaaS to sell.** Pip is the product. There are two top-level **modes** (toggle, `data-mode` on `<html>`, persisted `folio_mode`): **Work** (account management ŌĆö green) and **Life** (personal assistant ŌĆö dusty blue + a dusty-orange Pip: appointments, birthdays/events with a VIP heads-up ladder, honey-do). One app, one Pip brain spanning both; they unify in the daily brief. Hierarchy: **Work/Life mode ŌåÆ modules (Accounts, Gauge, ŌĆ” + Life) ŌåÆ workspaces (account slices, work-side only).** Build for the single user (Chris); keep RLS but don't add org-layer/multi-tenant overhead for hypothetical customers. (See item 42 + the June 10 handoff.)

**Folios is the umbrella product** ŌĆö a year-round account management app. Lanyard and Gauge are connected modules that live inside the Folios world, not separate apps with equal billing. The product name is **Folios** (plural); the GitHub repo is still named `Folio` (singular) for historical reasons ŌĆö don't rename the repo.

- **Folios** (`chrisvasconcellos97/Folio`) ŌĆö the main app. Year-round account management: accounts, meetings, cadences, contacts, open items, Pip AI. Production domain: `folioshq.com`. (Pipeline / revenue surfaces were intentionally ripped ŌĆö see "Ripped (deliberate simplification)" below.)
- **Lanyard** (separate repo) ŌĆö conference-specific module. Schedule, partner profiles, team chat, personal meeting notes, Pip AI. Punches out from Folios during conferences, feeds notes and partner data back.
- **Gauge** (lives under `gauge/` in this repo) ŌĆö project management module. Tracks commitments and deliverables from account meetings (Phase 1), then expands to company-wide product team integration where PMs manage work and AMs are linked to relevant projects (Phase 2). Feeds project status back into Folios account views.

All three share the **same Supabase project**: `https://yrpdjmyfidhxlpmxasao.supabase.co`

### Gauge ŌĆö Build Notes
- Phase 1: AM-facing. Commitments from meetings graduate into tracked projects in Gauge, visible on the account in Folios.
- Phase 2: Company-wide. Product team uses Gauge as their primary tool, AMs linked to relevant projects. Get input from OEC product team and PMs before building Phase 2 ŌĆö they'll know what's missing.
- Same security model as Folios and Lanyard ŌĆö shared Supabase, RLS, 2FA inherited automatically.

## Folios ŌĆö Current State

- React + Vite, deployed on Vercel at `folioshq.com`, live as of May 2026
- Supabase Auth (real email/password accounts)
- Tables: `folio_accounts`, `folio_contacts`, `folio_meetings`, `folio_items` ŌĆö all with RLS tied to `auth.uid()`. (Table names keep the `folio_` prefix ŌĆö they're DB identifiers, not user-facing brand.)
- `folio_meetings` has two extra columns added post-launch: `pip_summary text`, `pip_email text`
- Pip AI proxy at `api/pip.js` using `claude-haiku-4-5-20251001`, requires `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` in Vercel env vars
- Schema is in `supabase/schema.sql` ŌĆö run in production
- ABPA 2026 import is in `supabase/import_lanyard.sql` ŌĆö run in production
- 11 accounts and 8 meetings imported from Lanyard with Pip summaries and draft emails attached

## Lanyard ŌĆö Architecture Summary

- React + Vite, hosted on Vercel (separate deployment)
- **No real auth** ŌĆö uses anonymous user IDs (`lanyard_uid`) generated and stored in `localStorage`
- Supabase accessed via raw REST fetch calls (no SDK), anon key hardcoded in `App.jsx`
- Single-file app: `src/App.jsx` (~4300 lines)

### Storage pattern
- **Writes to localStorage immediately** for speed, then debounces a Supabase upsert 1.5 seconds later
- **On load**: checks Supabase first, falls back to localStorage if nothing found

### Supabase tables (Lanyard)

| Table | user_id value | What's stored |
|-------|--------------|---------------|
| `sessions` | `"abpa2026_team"` | Conference schedule events (shared) |
| `partners` | `"abpa2026_team"` | Partner/account profiles (shared) |
| `user_prefs` | `"u_<uid>"` | Hotel info, quick notes (personal) |
| `user_prefs` | `"u_<uid>_notes"` | Personal meeting notes per session (private) |
| `share_codes` | ŌĆö | Temporary codes for syncing between teammates |
| `notifications` | ŌĆö | Team activity feed (built, SQL not yet run) |
| `messages` | ŌĆö | Team chat, DMs, shoutouts (built, SQL not yet run) |

### The auth problem
`lanyard_uid` lives in localStorage ŌĆö clearing the browser or switching devices loses personal notes. Shared data (under `"abpa2026_team"`) is safe. **Adding real Supabase Auth to Lanyard is the top priority for the next Lanyard build.**

- Going forward, Lanyard will need real auth before bidirectional sync makes sense

## Pip

Both Folios and Lanyard use the same Pip personality ŌĆö a loyal, slightly anxious field analyst. Pip has access to account/meeting context injected into the system prompt. Model: `claude-haiku-4-5-20251001`.

### Pip cost strategy
- Generate Pip outputs once, save to DB (`pip_summary`, `pip_email` columns)
- Never regenerate what's already saved ŌĆö load from DB instead
- Future "Ask Pip" button should check for existing output before making an API call

### Pip operating context (June 10 2026)

`folio_user_profile.operating_context` holds the hand-authored distillation of THE INTERVIEW (the "Chris's Job ŌĆö Operating Context" section above, compressed to ~2.5k chars, data-line clean, includes the MSO not-his-relationships instruction). `useUserProfile` composes it ahead of `profile_prose`, so every client Pip surface inherits it with zero wiring; `generate-questions` and `operator-run` read it server-side directly. The periodic Q&A re-synthesis writes only `profile_prose` and can never clobber it. Update it via SQL when the interview's ground truth changes.

### Pip context parity rule
**Both Pip entrypoints must see the same data.** There are two places Pip is called:
1. **Ask Pip chat** ŌĆö `src/lib/pipContext.js` (`renderAccountFull`) + PipView.jsx
2. **Meeting summarize** ŌĆö `src/lib/pip.js` (`summarizeDraftPip`) + CadenceHub.jsx

Any new field added to the data model that should influence Pip's reasoning (new table, new column, new hook) must be wired to **both**. The pip_facts gap (folio_pip_facts only wired to chat, not summarize) was discovered in May 2026 and fixed ŌĆö this rule exists to prevent recurrence. When in doubt, grep for the field in both `pipContext.js` and `pip.js`.

## Supabase

- Project URL: `https://yrpdjmyfidhxlpmxasao.supabase.co`
- Same project for Folios and Lanyard
- Folios tables have proper RLS via `auth.uid()`
- Lanyard tables use text `user_id` fields (not auth UUIDs)

## Scalability Notes

This app is currently single-user but should be built with multi-tenancy in mind from the start. Every decision should assume it will eventually serve multiple businesses with multiple users per business.

- **RLS is already user-scoped** ŌĆö good foundation, but team/org layer will be needed
- **Future: add `org_id` to all tables** ŌĆö one org per business, users belong to orgs, RLS updates to match
- **Pip at scale** ŌĆö Haiku is cheap but at volume, saved outputs (never re-call for same meeting) are essential
- **Avoid hardcoding user IDs** ŌĆö `import_lanyard.sql` has a hardcoded user ID for one-time import only, never repeat this pattern in app code
- **Keep hooks thin** ŌĆö data logic lives in `/hooks`, components stay presentational
- **Schema changes** ŌĆö always add columns with `if not exists`, never destructive migrations

---

## Development Workflow

- Features requested by Chris go on **Pending Updates** list below
- Chris says "ship it" ŌåÆ everything on the list gets built in one batch
- Items drop off the list after they ship
- If items should be grouped for efficiency, suggest it before executing
- Never execute immediately on a feature request ŌĆö queue it first
- **Before shipping items 4ŌĆō7:** do a full layout audit first ŌĆö review placement, spacing, and information hierarchy across every screen to make sure new features land cleanly into a well-organized foundation

### Idea Capture Rule (read this every session)

**Nothing Chris mentions gets discarded.** Ideas have been lost across chats ŌĆö this is the fix.

- **Capture aggressively, not selectively.** If Chris says "could we also...", "what about...", "I'd love...", "I'm wondering if...", "would be nice to have...", or even floats a half-formed idea mid-conversation ŌåÆ it goes into **Pending Updates** or **Feature Wishlist / Roadmap** *that same turn*, before responding to anything else.
- **Even rejected/deferred ideas get logged** in the Wishlist with a one-line note on why deferred ŌĆö so they resurface if context changes.
- **Asides count.** "Side note, the Departments thing would be cool" ŌåÆ that's an idea, capture it.
- **Tangents in the middle of another feature discussion count.** If Chris is walking through Cadence Hub and mentions a Departments tab ŌåÆ capture Departments immediately, don't lose it in the Cadence Hub conversation.
- **When in doubt, log it.** A half-captured idea is recoverable. A forgotten idea is gone.
- **Confirm capture out loud** when you log something new mid-conversation: "Queued under [section]." So Chris sees it landed.

## ŌŁÉ CURRENT STATE & NEXT-JOB QUEUE (read this FIRST ŌĆö living doc, June 24 2026)

## Session Handoff ŌĆö June 19 2026 (F5): Pip chat agent loop ŌĆö the last FORM item (SHIPPED June 20)

**ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ STATE CHANGE ŌĆö F5 is LIVE on `main` / `folioshq.com` (shipped June 20, first of the three-feature push).** Chris said "push all to main"; F5 was rebased onto `main` (CLAUDE.md conflict resolved), gates re-run green (345 tests), pushed (`115deda ŌåÆ 53795e1`). No DB changes (code + docs only). Kill switch if it ever misbehaves: `PIP_AGENT_LOOP=off` in Vercel (instant, no redeploy).

**DONE ŌĆö F5, the last X6 FORM item (F1/F2/F3/F5 now done; F6 built, awaiting a key).** Chat was single-shot: the model answered in one pass, the client ran any action, and the tool result never returned to the model. F5 makes chat a real **agent loop** ŌĆö model emits a READ tool ŌåÆ server executes it (RLS-scoped, JWT) ŌåÆ `tool_result` ŌåÆ model continues ŌåÆ final answer. Multi-step in one turn ("find the stalled project, then draft the chase note").

**The build (no-regression by construction ŌĆö the #1 rule):**
- **NEW `src/lib/pipAgentTools.js`** (pure, 15 tests) ŌĆö read-only tool defs + loop control: `isReadTool`, `partitionToolUses`, `decideLoopStep`, `buildToolResultBlocks`.
- **NEW `api/_pipAgentLoop.js`** (server I/O; receives the client as a param so it stays outside Guard 3) ŌĆö `executeReadTool` (Supabase via caller JWT, **writes nothing**) + `runAgentChat` (drives the loop, streams deltas live).
- **`api/pip.js`** ŌĆö chat (stream + buffered) routes through `runAgentChat` when enabled.
- **THREE read tools (read-only, own-notebook only):** `lookup_account` (deep single-account read, rendered via the F1 shared `src/lib/accountContext.js` surface:"chat" ŌåÆ parity by construction) ┬Ę `find_open_work(filter)` (overdue/stalled/waiting_on_them/due_soon/all) ┬Ę `search_notes(query)` (ilike over meeting notes + Pip summaries ŌĆö plain text, NOT pgvector; that's F6).
- **No-regression design:** existing action tools (`pipTools.js`) UNCHANGED + terminal (still go to the client confirm-card path); the loop only READS, never commits. A turn is either gathering (read tools ŌåÆ loop continues) or acting (action tool ŌåÆ terminate, hand to client). Read tools never cross to the client. **Degrades to single-shot by construction** ŌĆö no read tool emitted ŌåÆ exactly one model call ŌåÆ byte-identical to today. Kill switch `PIP_AGENT_LOOP=off` removes read tools entirely (instant, no redeploy).
- **Cost guard:** Ōēż4 model calls/turn (`PIP_AGENT_MAX_STEPS`, default 4); the last allowed step forces `tool_choice:{type:"none"}` ŌåÆ clean text answer, never a half-finished loop. `logPipUsage` fires per model call (spend tile sees the full looped-turn cost). Worst case ~$0.01ŌĆō0.03 only on a fully-looped turn; most turns = 1 call.
- **Invariants held:** prompt cache (tools + system byte-stable across iterations; only `messages` grows) ┬Ę streaming preserved (deltas stream across iterations; `pipStream.js` + PipView UNCHANGED ŌĆö loop is fully server-internal) ┬Ę Data Line clean (reads Chris's own verbatim notebook; tools never solicit numbers, never retain).

**Gates green:** `vite build` Ō£ō ┬Ę **345 tests** (330 + 15 new) Ō£ō ┬Ę `check-guards` (6) Ō£ō ┬Ę `test-api-imports` Ō£ō. Commits: `13adeb1` (plan) ┬Ę `a4542b4` (tools + control logic) ┬Ę `1d1e736` (server loop) ┬Ę `3173741` (docs/PDFs). Plan doc: `docs/pip-architecture-f5-plan.md`.

**Sanity-Pass caveat (green build ŌēĀ proof ŌĆö the modelŌåötool round-trip isn't unit-testable, only the control logic is). Chris's live spot-check before FF:** (1) multi-step: *"what's stalled, and draft a nudge for the worst one"* ŌåÆ should call `find_open_work` then answer with a draft in one turn; (2) deep read: ask about an account NOT in context ŌåÆ should `lookup_account` instead of asking you to narrow; (3) no regression: normal chat + an action ("mark the CAPA item done" ŌĆö still shows the confirm card) behave exactly as today. If anything misbehaves: `PIP_AGENT_LOOP=off` in Vercel (instant kill).

**Still open (X6 FORM):** F6 = pgvector semantic recall ŌĆö now SHIPPED to `main` (see F6 handoff below); needs `OPENAI_API_KEY` in Vercel to activate. F1/F2/F3/F5/F6 all done.

## Session Handoff ŌĆö June 19 2026 (F6): pgvector semantic recall ŌĆö Pip recalls by MEANING (SHIPPED June 19)

**ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ STATE CHANGE ŌĆö F6 is LIVE on `main` / `folioshq.com` (shipped June 19 alongside F5 + the Monday pack).** Chris said "push all to main"; the F6 branch was rebased onto main (docs-only conflicts resolved), gates re-run green, pushed. **INERT until `OPENAI_API_KEY` is added to Vercel** ŌĆö degrades cleanly to recency-only context, no errors. The `folio_embeddings` table + `match_folio_embeddings` RPC + `vector` extension were already applied to prod (additive).

**DONE ŌĆö F6, the last memory-architecture step.** Pip's per-account context used to only show the *latest* N meetings by date; older decisions/constraints were invisible. F6 adds **semantic recall**: Pip pulls the most *relevant* past notes by meaning. It plugs into F1's shared `buildAccountContext()` ŌĆö a new `recall` section ŌĆö so it reaches chat by construction (parity rule).

**The build (plan-first per the F1/F3 playbook ŌĆö `docs/pip-architecture-f6-plan.md`):**
- **Schema** (`supabase/folio_embeddings.sql` + `schema.sql`): `folio_embeddings` (user_id, source_type, source_id, account_id, chunk, `content_fingerprint`, `embedding vector(1536)`, RLS on `auth.uid()`, **hnsw** cosine index). `match_folio_embeddings(...)` RPC ŌĆö **SECURITY INVOKER + explicit `user_id = auth.uid()` predicate** (belt + suspenders), always called with the user-JWT client.
- **Embed seam** (`api/_embed.js`): OpenAI `text-embedding-3-small` (1536d) via plain `fetch`, **key-optional** (no key ŌåÆ returns null ŌåÆ everything no-ops). `toVectorLiteral()` passes pgvector its `[...]` text form (de-risks the PostgRESTŌåÆvector cast).
- **Writer** (`api/embed-sync.js`): loads meeting notes/summaries/project-notes/account-updates (RLS), **fingerprint-gates per source** (embed-once), one batched OpenAI call, delete-then-insert chunks. Logs embed spend. Registered in `test-api-imports.js`.
- **Trigger** (`src/hooks/useEmbeddingSync.js`): once/day/user, fire-and-forget. Called above App's `authLoading` return (Hook Order Rule); no-ops without userId/accounts/key.
- **Reader** (`api/pip.js#attachRecall`): embeds the question, runs the RPC per focused account or one global lane in list mode. Gated chat/brief + Ōēź12-char query + key present; fail-silent. **Render** in the shared builder: `accountContext.js` new `recall` section (on for chat/brief, OFF for summarize/operator ŌĆö can opt in later) + `pipContext.js` global lane.
- **Docs:** `data-handling.md` (what's embedded + RLS + the OpenAI boundary) ┬Ę `ai-governance.md` ┬Ę `product-overview.md` ┬Ę `upgrades.md` ┬Ę fixlist F6 ticked ┬Ę PDFs.

**DATA LINE (compliance):** embeds only the user's own notes (verbatim) + Pip's already-generalized `pip_summary` (no NEW number retention). RLS-scoped to the user, account-scoped by default. OpenAI is a new boundary, documented.

**Gates green:** `vite build` Ō£ō ┬Ę tests Ō£ō (8 new: 5 accountContext recall, 3 pipContext recall) ┬Ę `check-guards` (6) Ō£ō ┬Ę `test-api-imports` Ō£ō.

**ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ CHRIS ŌĆö TO ACTIVATE F6:** (1) **Add `OPENAI_API_KEY` to Vercel env** ŌĆö recall is INERT without it. Optional `PIP_EMBED_MODEL` override. (2) **Live spot-check (Sanity-Pass ŌĆö green build ŌēĀ proof):** after the key's in + a day's sweep (or hit `/api/embed-sync` once), ask Pip a chat question whose answer lives in an OLD meeting ŌåÆ it should surface a "RELEVANT PAST NOTES" block. The PostgRESTŌåÆ`vector` cast is the one path not exercised without a live JWT (de-risked via text-literal form). If recall returns nothing: key set? embed-sync ran (rows in `folio_embeddings`)? RPC returns under the user's JWT?

**Still open (Chris's call ŌĆö out of F6 scope):** after-summarize instant-embed trigger; recall inside summarize/operator (section exists, default-off). Operator-run cost levers (item 48 #4/#5/#6) still open.

## Session Handoff ŌĆö June 19 2026 (F3): event-driven Pip-state recompute ŌĆö the 70ŌĆō90% cost cut (SHIPPED June 19)

**ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ STATE CHANGE ŌĆö F3 is LIVE on `main` / `folioshq.com` (shipped in `c93f2f1`).** Chris said "just push it"; `main` fast-forwarded cleanly from `claude/f3-pip-event-recompute-sxllsa`, gates re-run green (330 tests), one Vercel prod deploy went out. The 3-column migration was already on prod. (Original framing below said "branch, NOT deployed" ŌĆö that's now stale; left for the record. Spot-check still worth doing per the live-check note below.)

**DONE ŌĆö F2 + F3, the audit's headline Pip-cost job.** Pip's per-account "state" read (where it stands / momentum / risks) was refreshed on **timers** (a 6h background pass over top accounts + another sweep every time Pip chat opened) whether or not anything changed ŌĆö tokens burned to re-describe unchanged accounts. The old change-gate watched only `last_interaction_at`, so it ALSO missed task closes/edits (a staleness leak). F3 makes recompute **event-driven**; F2 persists the structured context F1 produced so the gate has something stable to compare against.

**The build (two-tier gate):**
- **Tier 1 ŌĆö client (`src/App.jsx` Part 9 rewritten):** no more timers. Recomputes an account only when a real signal ŌĆö `max(last_interaction_at, meeting.updated_at, task.updated_at)` ŌĆö is newer than `context_checked_at` (last eval). Widens triggers meeting-only ŌåÆ meeting + task add/close/edit. In-flight ref guards realtime thrash; Major-tier first; batch capped at 20. Removed PipView's redundant chat-open sweep (one sweep ŌĆö App Coherence).
- **Tier 2 ŌĆö server (`api/pip-state-refresh.js`):** rebuilds a content fingerprint and **skips the Haiku call entirely when nothing changed ($0)**; `force` flag bypasses (manual "resync Pip memory" button).
- **F2 foundation (persisted):** new columns on `folio_pip_account_state` ŌĆö `context_struct` (jsonb), `context_fingerprint` (text), `context_checked_at` (timestamptz). New pure helper `computeContextFingerprint()` in `src/lib/accountContext.js` hashes **STABLE inputs only** (ids/dates/counts, never relative-time) so it can't drift daily. +7 tests incl. the "+1 day = same hash" drift lock.

**Why it's safe (Sanity-Pass):** fingerprint computed **server-side only** ŌåÆ no client/server divergence trap; Haiku prompt input unchanged ŌåÆ `state_prose` quality identical, just fresher on real change; **fails toward freshness** (false positive = $0 skip; never skips when in doubt). **Result: ~70ŌĆō90% fewer per-account refresh AI calls, no freshness loss (actually fresher ŌĆö task changes now trigger it).**

**Gates:** `vite build` Ō£ō ┬Ę **330 tests** (323 + 7 new) Ō£ō ┬Ę `check-guards` (6) Ō£ō ┬Ę `test-api-imports` Ō£ō. Commits: `25ed1b8` (plan) ┬Ę `ee0046f` (F2 + F3 server) ┬Ę `61c3fe7` (F3 client) ┬Ę `6cd3b1b` (docs/upgrades/fixlist). Design doc: `docs/pip-architecture-f3-plan.md`. Migration: `supabase/pip_context_fingerprint.sql` + folded into `schema.sql`.

**Live spot-check to do (Chris, before fast-forwarding `main`):** (1) summarize a meeting or close a task on an account, then open Pip chat there ŌĆö its read should reflect the change (gate fired); (2) open chat on an *untouched* account twice ŌĆö second open should NOT re-bill (fingerprint skip). Then `git push origin claude/f3-pip-event-recompute-sxllsa:main` ŌåÆ one Vercel deploy.

**Still open (Chris's call ŌĆö out of F3 scope):** retiring the Haiku `state_prose` ENTIRELY (bigger cut but changes what reaches the chat model ŌĆö deferred); operator-run cost levers (item 48 #4/#5/#6 ŌĆö conditional output fields, on-demand draft emails, skip roll-up on quiet nights).

## Session Handoff ŌĆö June 18 2026 (F1): ONE shared buildAccountContext() ŌĆö the tri-renderer drift cured (SHIPPED June 19 ŌĆö see handoff above)

**ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ WHERE IT LIVES:** branch **`claude/app-audit-strategy-hhcrz2-4ix1ho`** (pushed, 5 commits), **NOT `main`, NOT deployed.** Chris asked to build on the branch and NOT ship until he tests it himself ŌĆö the deploy-to-`main` rule was explicitly suspended for this session at his instruction. He fast-forwards `main` after testing. No DB changes, no migrations pending.

F1 collapses them into ONE shared builder so adding a field reaches every surface by construction.

**The build (one surface per commit, each gated with `vite build` + `vitest` + `check-guards` + `test-api-imports`):**
- **NEW `src/lib/accountContext.js`** ŌĆö pure module (NO supabase/React/fetch, so chat+summarize client AND operator-run server all import it). Exports `buildAccountContext(account, opts)` ŌåÆ structured `{sections:[{key,text,spaced}]}` and `renderAccountContext(account, opts)` ŌåÆ prose. `account` = merged per-account bundle (scalars + nested arrays). `opts.surface` Ōłł `chat|brief|summarize|operator` selects a preset in a single **`SURFACE_DEFAULTS`** map ŌĆö the intentional per-surface omissions + depth now live in ONE reviewable place (parity rule: wire a field to both, but surface-appropriate trimming stays explicit).
- **Routed all three:** chat/brief (`pipContext.renderContextProse` ŌåÆ builder, deleted `renderAccountFull` + 5 helpers + the `computeContactEngagement` import) ┬Ę summarize (`pip.js summarizeDraftPip` bp3 ŌåÆ builder, deleted 7 render helpers; **cache breakpoints preserved** ŌĆö BP1 static rules untouched, account context stays the BP3 per-account cached layer, meeting history moved BP4ŌåÆBP3 since it's account-stable; summarize-specific blocks stay caller-side: routing roster, internal/person framing, people directory, cadence schedule, correction read-back, BP4 working set with I-/T-/project ids) ┬Ę operator-run (`api/operator-run.js` now imports the shared module ŌĆö traded the "self-contained, no src/lib imports" property for the parity guarantee; `.js`-extension chain + api-imports bundle test verified; deleted the local renderer + orphaned `excerpt()`).
- **Drift lock:** **`src/lib/accountContext.test.js`** (25 tests) ŌĆö feeds ONE fixed bundle, asserts each surface emits every field it needs AND cross-checks parity-class fields (ownership, waiting_on, promise log, operator read, systems) reach >1 surface. A future edit that drops a field from one path fails CI.

**PRESERVED, not rebuilt ŌĆö last session's parity fixes** (they're now FIELDS in the shared builder, asserted by the parity tests): globalPeopleŌåÆchat, operator-stateŌåÆsummarize, waiting_onŌåÆbriefs, health/promise into chat, ownership awareness, data-line guards.

**F4 (cache) within scope:** static system blocks left byte-stable; builder output is the per-account cached tail. No speculative `cache_control` changes (would risk behavior without a live test).

**Validation:** `vite build` Ō£ō ┬Ę **323 tests** (298 baseline + 25 new) Ō£ō ┬Ę `check-guards` Ō£ō ┬Ę `test-api-imports` Ō£ō (confirms operator-run's new `../src/lib/accountContext.js` import resolves in the serverless bundle). Mirrors this session's quick-assign-chip scoping ŌåÆ the whole person-picker is now coherent (App Coherence Rule). Mechanics: each group tagged `scope: "primary"|"team"|"other"`; `canScope = primaryIds.length > 0 && hasOther` (an account-less picker shows everyone, unchanged); a selected value outside the scoped set (`valueIsOther`) force-opens the full list so it stays visible/selected; `__showall__` is a UI-only expander (never changes `value`). Gates green: `vite build` ┬Ę 323 tests ┬Ę check-guards ┬Ę test-api-imports. No schema/docs changes (internal UI polish). ## Session Handoff ŌĆö June 18 2026 (LATE): DEPLOYED TO PROD + triplication bug fixed + F1 plan written

5. **Writers ŌåÆ folio_tasks** ŌĆö new `src/lib/projectTaskWrites.js#reconcileProjectTasks` (diffs a stage array ŌåÆ folio_tasks insert/update/delete by id, sort_order=position). Routed through it: `ProjectStageEditor.commitStages`, `CadenceHub` HubProjectCard, `StandingBoardView`, `MyQueueView`, `ProjectModal` save. `pipPlanApply` new_taskŌåÆ`addItem(project_id)` / update_taskŌåÆ`updateItem` by id. `ItemsTab` escalateŌåÆ`insertTask`. `GaugeView` toggle: dropped the stale stages-sync bridge, recompute status from tasks. Shared `firstStatusColumn` + `stageToTaskFields` helpers; `userId` threaded to the editors.
6. **Parity + docs** ŌĆö verified (above); `docs/upgrades.md` entry, fixlist ┬¦4/┬¦10 ticked, `schema.sql` header updated, PDFs regenerated.

## Session Handoff ŌĆö June 17 2026: Summarize UX + Pip orb everywhere + operator goes manual + iOS TTS

**Where things stand:** production (`folioshq.com`) is current through `e3cdd63` on `main` and live. No schema migrations this session ŌĆö all code-only. The arc, shipped in several pushes:

**iOS TTS (the opening thread).** Pip's voice was totally silent on iOS. Root-caused on-device (persistent debug panel, since removed): Kokoro's `_tts.generate()` **hangs forever on iOS** (82M ONNX model blows the Safari tab-memory cap ŌĆö no resolve, no throw), so the catch/fallback never ran. Rebuilt the playback path: **WebAudio AudioBuffer built directly from Kokoro's PCM** (no `decodeAudioData`; WebAudio also ignores the Ring/Silent switch, unlike HTMLAudioElement), gesture-time AudioContext unlock + keep-alive, speechSynthesis primed in the gesture, and a **15s timeout on generate ŌåÆ system-voice fallback**. Net: desktop gets the real Kokoro voice; **mobile falls back to the iOS system voice** (Daniel ŌĆö Chris dislikes it; the real fix is server-side Kokoro, still parked). `src/lib/useKokoroTTS.js`.

**Pip summarize ŌĆö temperature + the "confusing/complex" UX overhaul.** (1) **Temperature 0.3** on `summary` mode in `api/pip.js` (was API-default ~1.0 ŌĆö the cause of "great once, nonsense usually"); env-overridable via `PIP_SUMMARY_TEMPERATURE`; threaded as `cfg.temperature` only where a mode opts in. (2) **Scannable rows** ŌĆö `PipSummarizePreview` rows now render as a one-liner (task text + meta chips: kind ┬Ę Ō£”commitment ┬Ę due ┬Ę ŌåÆaccount) with an **Edit** toggle; the full control stack (assignee/recipient/due/account/project/source) is unchanged but hidden until expanded (`expandedRows` state). Receipts ("What Pip used") collapsed by default. (3) **Pip suggests projects** ŌĆö the missing half: `SUMMARIZE_SCHEMA_RULES` now emits a shared `suggested_project_title` on Ōēź2 new_item rows that form one coherent NEW initiative (conservative ŌĆö most meetings suggest none); `normalizePlanRow` passes it through; the preview groups them into a one-tap "Ō£” Pip suggests a project ŌĆö Create & file" banner that creates the Gauge project and routes those rows in via `gaugeProjectId`. (4) **Ad-hoc parity** ŌĆö `AdHocConversationFlow` now passes `onCreateProject` so one-off conversations get the same project controls as cadence meetings. **VERIFY ON DEVICE:** that suggestion-linked items land where Chris expects in Gauge (folio_tasks.project_id vs stages dual-model ŌĆö flagged, not yet confirmed).

**Pip orb ŌĆö new 3D form everywhere (Visual Spec Rule sign-off, in-session).** Cutoff lowered **mdŌåÆ3D** (`md`=32px floor; only the tiny Ōēż22px `xs`/`sm` inline marks stay classic) ŌĆö fixes "Pip chat has the old orb" + cards/status banners. Home **hero orb is now clickable ŌåÆ opens Pip chat** (`onOpenPip`). **Speaking ring "zigzag"** added: `PIP_SPEC.speakingRingAmp/Freq/Speed` + optional `speakAmp` arg to `buildPipFrame` (idle passes 0 ŌåÆ byte-identical ŌåÆ **53-test drift lock still passes**); tuned to a subtle tight shimmer (amp 0.03, freq 11, speed 5) after Chris said the first cut "looked like it's dancing." **Floating Pip removed** ŌĆö bottom-right orb gone on Home (desktop) and on ALL mobile screens (Pip lives in the nav now); **nav-bar Pip lowered** (`marginTop -12ŌåÆ-2`) so it sits in the bar. Both the cutoff + speaking-state changes recorded in the Pip Visual Spec Rule.

**Pip operator ŌĆö RETIRED THE NIGHTLY CRON, now manual-trigger only.** Per Chris's cost decision (it runs every morning whether or not he opens the app; the report "rarely changes his day"): removed the `crons` entry from `vercel.json`. `api/operator-run.js` now accepts **either** the cron secret (privileged) **or a valid Supabase user JWT** (scopes the run strictly to that user ŌĆö the browser button can't hold the cron secret). New `OperatorRunButton` on Home (`src/views/home/OperatorRunButton.jsx`): authenticates with the user's session token, ~20-40s working state, refetches the report on completion; renders as a prompt card when there's no report today, a subtle "Ōå╗ Refresh" when there is. **Knowledge is unaffected** ŌĆö the operator pass *reads* memory, doesn't write it; daily health snapshots are written on app-open, not by the pass. Brief auto-advance bug fixed in the same arc: the Start-My-Day brief advances on `speaking` trueŌåÆfalse, but the system-voice fallback never set `speaking=true`, so it froze on "Your word" ŌĆö new `fallbackSpeak()` drives the state, and Kokoro is marked failed-for-session after one timeout so later cards skip the 15s wait.

**"Is Folios earning its keep?" ŌĆö new read-only dashboard** (top of Settings ŌåÆ Pip). `useFolioHealth` reads `folio_pip_usage` + `pip_correction_log` + `folio_meetings` (account stats from accounts in memory) ŌåÆ feed-rate (days fed / accounts touched-vs-cold), accuracy (corrections last 14d + trend + top type), a canary (flags the operator run if silent Ōēź3d), cost (30d + top spender + week-over-week), and a deterministic one-line verdict. No new tables, no writes, no Pip calls; fails soft to "ŌĆö".

Uses the service-role admin client with explicit `user_id` filter ŌĆö correct under RLS bypass. ### Phase 0 ŌĆö Hardening ŌĆö Ō£ģ SHIPPED June 10 2026 PM (commits 13fb1f5 + 2fb097b + d246256 on main)
