- **Bugs:** `api/ask-pip.js` raw-JSON-on-truncation (copy portfolio-brief's regex-salvage + check `stop_reason`); `api/operator-run.js` silent empty operator state on JSON parse failure (log raw output to console/`folio_errors`); un-suppress commitment nudges when operator report active (`HomeView.jsx` ~line 1236); dead "Open brief ŌåÆ" pill when no calls today (~line 1020); ISO date leaking into draft-ahead card.
- **Safety nets:** add `npm run test` to `.github/workflows/ci.yml`; write tests for `accountHealth.js` + `pipPlanApply.js` (+ `lifeLadder.js` later); register `api/invite.js` in `scripts/test-api-imports.js`; attach JWT to `profile-synthesis.js` client (latent footgun).
- **API guards:** server rate-limit on `portfolio-brief.js`; `export const config = { maxDuration: 60 }` on `portfolio-brief.js` + `business-review.js`; truncation detection in `leadership-readout.js`; `generate-questions.js` model failures ŌåÆ 500 (not 200-with-modelError).
- **Performance:** lazy-load `AccountDetail` + `StartConversationModal` + `AddAccountModal` + `PipCatchUp` (cuts ~150ŌĆō200 kB off the 670 kB index chunk); dynamic-import `pip.js` out of App.jsx (only `compressCorrectionsPip` used); `.limit()` on global `useMeetings` + size-guard its localStorage cache; fix `CadenceMeetingMode` ESC-handler re-registration on every keystroke (useRef); reduce cold-open queries ~27ŌåÆ~15 (move `fetchAllContacts`/`fetchAllUpdates` into AccountDetail; collapse drip-question triple query; pass in-memory data to `computeAndSaveSnapshots`).

### Success criteria (~3 months out ŌĆö check these, don't vibe them)
1. Chris opens Folios at 9am and in <60s knows what he owes, what's today, and has answered Pip's Ōēż3 check-in questions ŌĆö and the corrected report is accurate.
2. No flat-footed Mondays ŌĆö the 1:1 pack means nothing the boss raises is a surprise.
3. Most meeting summaries apply with zero cleanup; task counts are small and right.
4. The email/Teams day reaches Folios daily via the digest, and it shows ŌĆö account pages worth opening, chat worth asking.
5. Chris never maintains the same information in two places by hand ŌĆö the team sheet is generated from Folios (export + reminder loop); the drift problem is dead.

If any criterion stays false, that's where we dig next ŌĆö design failure, not user failure (especially #4: if the digest habit doesn't stick in 3 weeks, redesign the friction, don't blame the habit).

**51. Pip intelligence roadmap (TIER 1 ŌĆö accuracy/trust; see consolidated tier map above) ŌĆö "feed Pip more reality before making it a better thinker" (QUEUED June 24 2026, from a 3-round ClaudeŌåöChatGPT design exchange Chris ran)** ŌĆö *(NOT built ŌĆö captured so it doesn't die in chat. Chris bounced "how does Pip work / how to improve him" off ChatGPT across 3 rounds; the two AIs converged hard. This is the distilled, de-duped roadmap + the decisions already locked. Build order is MINE (Claude's) recommendation, greenlit-pending. NOTE post-consolidation: 1b "end-of-day brain dump" now lives under item 52(A) as the canonical capture-inbox home ŌĆö it's a scheduled trigger on that inbox, not a separate build.)* The unifying insight (the one I'd weight above everything): **the binding constraint is the CAPTURE GAP ŌĆö Pip only sees ~10% of Chris's day ŌĆö so reasoning upgrades have a ceiling until more reality is in. Prioritize capture at least as highly as smarter reasoning.** The bundle, in recommended order:
   - **(1a) Explainable health** ŌĆö never just "At Risk"; always "At Risk *because* ŌĆö no substantive touch 24d ┬Ę supplier owes May follow-up ┬Ę implementation project inactive." **We already COMPUTE these signals in `gatherSignals` (accountHealth.js) and throw them away** ŌĆö this is surfacing existing data, near-zero effort, biggest trust win per hour. Account health pill caption + Pip's health language both read the reasons. **Effort S.**
   - **(1b) End-of-day brain dump** ŌĆö a 4:30pm nudge: "Anything happen today that isn't in here?" ŌåÆ free-text ŌåÆ Pip structures + files it. **Reuses `QuickCaptureModal` + `api/parse-digest` wholesale** (it's quick-capture on a daily trigger with multi-row parse). Highest capture-gap recovery per minute; cheap. **Effort S.** *(1a + 1b are the bundle I'd ship FIRST ŌĆö small, compounding, touch nothing risky.)*
   - **(2a) Counter-evidence before any "stalled/dropped" alarm** ŌĆö before Pip cries fire, it must search for evidence AGAINST the alarm (recent note / digest mention / related project moved) and downgrade confidence if found. **This IS the All Star Monday bug** ("work done over the weekend, just unmarked; Pip screamed overdue-fire"). Uses retrieval we already have (semantic recall + `search_notes`). Complements the existing personal-baseline anomaly check + the two-way morning check-in. **Effort M.**
   - **(2b) Ownership inference from notes** ŌĆö auto-extract "waiting on John since [date]" from *"John said he'd get back next week"* at summarize time, instead of manual `waiting_on` flags. The real "who has the ball" upgrade. **DECISION LOCKED: evidence-backed, NO decay-math / NO fabricated confidence %** (both AIs agreed 0.82ŌåÆ0.35 is invented precision that fights the staleness-humility work). Surface it as evidence + elapsed-time ("waiting on John ┬Ę he said next week ┬Ę 18d, no mention since"), which is what the aged board already does honestly. **Effort M.**
   - **(3) Commitment confidence buckets in summarize** ŌĆö classify extracted lines as explicit commitment / likely / discussion-point so "we talked about reporting" never becomes a task. Prompt-level sharpening of the precision-over-volume doctrine + existing `is_commitment` flag. **Effort S** (watch it doesn't just add UI noise).
   - **(4) Soft-structured digest (handoff format upgrade)** ŌĆö keep the digest paste FREE-FORM (the #49 de-brand explicitly rejected rigid `[OWE]/[WAITING]` tags ŌĆö do not regress that), but make work-Claude's prose follow a *predictable shape* and make Pip's EXTRACTION richer: pull sentiment / stakeholder-changes / momentum / risk, not just owe/waiting/touch. Richer output schema, NOT a stiffer input contract. **Effort M.**
   - **(5) Relationship facts ŌĆö EVIDENCE-ONLY, computed-over-inferred** ŌĆö store only traceable facts: recurring-theme counts ("onboarding raised 4├Ś"), commitment history (made/kept-on-time/missed ŌĆö **this is a COUNT from the promise log, not a judgment**), role evolution. **DECISION LOCKED: do NOT persist soft traits** (trust/influence/communication-style) ŌĆö both AIs agreed an inferred "Mike is unreliable" becomes a lens that compounds bias. **Effort L.**
   - **(6) Account Narrative Memory ŌĆö the high-ceiling / high-risk one, build LAST** ŌĆö a persisted "story of the relationship" (began at integration ŌåÆ strong early ŌåÆ slowed on resource constraints ŌåÆ renewed interest ŌåÆ hinges on onboarding). Maps onto Chris's core need ("I can't problem-solve unless I know the account cold"). **CRITICAL DESIGN DECISION (mine, neither AI caught it): build it RE-DERIVED, not ACCUMULATING.** An accreting narrative has the EXACT bias-lock failure ChatGPT itself flagged for traits, one level up ŌĆö a wrong "supplier is resource-constrained" becomes a lens over the whole account. So: re-derive the arc from evidence on each material change (the F3 event-driven pattern, extended to a longitudinal read), keep `folio_account_snapshots` as the evidence floor so it can always be rebuilt vs. blindly trusted, and **extend the existing account-state read rather than add a parallel narrative table** (App Coherence ŌĆö no second drifting store). **Effort L.** Earns its spot last, after the cheap accuracy/capture wins prove out.
   - **REJECTED (don't resurrect):** clipboard watcher (compliance landmine ŌĆö slurps raw corporate email/numbers; also browser clipboard needs a paste gesture; manual paste already exists); fabricated confidence percentages anywhere (fights staleness-humility); rigid-tag digest template (regresses #49). **VALIDATED current architecture:** event-driven account state + meeting-specific retrieval is right ŌĆö do NOT build a giant always-on full-history context (token explosion + stale reasoning).

**52. The Mastermind / Synthesis layer ŌĆö Pip connects the dots across the fire hose (QUEUED June 24 2026, Chris's vision ŌĆö the PAYOFF that makes the capture habit worth it)** ŌĆö *(NOT built ŌĆö captured + being designed with Chris. This is the thesis that ties item 51 together: now that Chris is feeding daily email digests + stray captures, he wants Pip to SYNTHESIZE the stream over time, not just file rows. His words: "if I give him 3 days in a row of 'Tara at LKQ is going to give me account numbers for X shops,' I want him to realize I keep bringing this up and offer to DO something ŌĆö build a Gauge project? chase it? ŌĆö that's the level of thinking I want. He should scan all this and piece things together." + "what if I had ONE spot to shove info in and Pip becomes a mastermind that sees it all and makes suggestions.")*
   - **ŌŁÉ NORTH STAR (the FEELING, not the mechanics ŌĆö Chris, June 24 2026, articulating the bar he can't fully spec):** "I want it to seriously feel like Pip is a genius reading everything and feeding it into each accountŌĆ” Pip should basically be me in thereŌĆ” someone should be blown away by what Pip can produce." What he's actually describing is an EXPERIENCE, not a feature ŌĆö decoded into three layers, in BUILD ORDER (this ordering is the strategy, not just a list): **(1) The river reaches every faucet** ŌĆö everything Chris dumps must SATURATE each account's context, so the cadence brief / pre-call brief / account state already KNOW what he fed Pip in his summaries. The pipes exist (F1 shared `buildAccountContext`, F2 persisted, F3 event-driven recompute, F6 recall) ŌĆö the work is making the capture stream actually flow through them richly (relationship texture + momentum + "what we talked about last time," not just filed tasks). This is the FOUNDATION; the suggestions are a bolt-on without it. **(2) The instant pre-call brief is the "blown-away" moment** ŌĆö Chris's own example ("jumping on a call, need a brief quick ŌåÆ last time they emailed you talked about X"). Tap one button ŌåÆ *where you stand ┬Ę last contact you discussed X ┬Ę you owe Y ┬Ę they've gone quiet on Z ┬Ę the one thing to raise is W.* Specific, grounded in his own words, ~10s. This single surface, done well, IS the "someone's blown away" demo ŌĆö it's not a dashboard, it's Pip handing him his own brain back, caught up, on demand. **(3) THEN the proactive mastermind suggestions** (the A/B halves below). **WHY THIS ORDER = the answer to "I don't want the first proposal to be WTF":** grounded surfaces (briefs that QUOTE his reality back) literally CAN'T produce a WTF ŌĆö they're not guessing, they're reciting what he said. Start there, earn trust that Pip reads the room correctly, and ONLY THEN do the bolder "you keep mentioning Tara ŌĆö make a project?" suggestions land as genius instead of noise. You earn "genius" by starting grounded, not by starting big. If only the pre-call brief shipped well, the north-star feeling is already mostly delivered; the mastermind is the encore, not the opening act.
   - **(A) One capture inbox ŌĆö "shove anything in here."** Elevate quick-capture into THE always-available brain-dump: the daily email digest AND stray one-liners ("just spoke with Dan, he's getting me a new file to upload") go to the same place. Every line is filed by kind (task/waiting/touch) AND retained as a lightweight signal the synthesis pass reasons over. Reuses `QuickCaptureModal` + `api/parse-digest`. Answer to Chris's "should I throw info in even if it's not on the summary?" ŌåÆ **YES, that's the whole point** ŌĆö the more reality in, the smarter the synthesis (item 51's capture-gap thesis).
   - **(B) The synthesis pass ŌĆö the actual "mastermind."** A periodic (daily / event-gated, NOT always-on) Sonnet pass over recent stream items (tasks, captures, digest rows, waiting-ons, recent notes) that detects **recurrence + convergence + stalls** and emits a SMALL set of high-confidence proactive suggestions. The four patterns worth surfacing: (1) **same pending thing mentioned N days running** (Tara/account-numbers ├Ś3) ŌåÆ "you keep raising this ŌĆö promote to a Gauge project? chase it? it's been open 6d"; (2) **a promise that recurs but never closes** = a stall signal ŌåÆ chase/escalate; (3) **convergent theme across accounts** ("file upload" with Dan AND Tara ŌåÆ maybe a process problem, not two account problems); (4) **a waiting-on that's gone quiet past the account's own rhythm**. Pip PROPOSES, Chris approves (one-tap ŌåÆ creates the project / chase note / waiting-on). 
   - **CAPABILITY MENU ŌĆö the "level of ability" Chris wants (June 24 2026 ŌĆö these are illustrations of the BAR, not a build list; the assignee example in item 54 was just one of many). The unifying mechanism in every one: stream + memory ŌåÆ a SPECIFIC, GROUNDED move Chris didn't ask for. Clerk ŌåÆ chief of staff.** Grouped by type of thinking:
     - **Connect threads across time/accounts:** "3 suppliers flagged the same product-team delay this week ŌĆö that's one product problem, not three account problems; draft a boss summary?" ┬Ę "'onboarding friction' has hit LKQ 4├Ś in 6 weeks and never resolved ŌĆö it's becoming the thing the account hinges on." ┬Ę "two stalled projects both wait on the same product person ŌĆö one conversation unblocks both."
     - **Walk into every call caught up (pre-call brief, full form):** "call with Tara in 20 min ŌĆö last email you owed her the shop file, doesn't look sent; top of your brief." ┬Ę "LKQ Thursday ŌĆö last two meetings you gave timelines that slipped, they'll ask; here's where it really stands."
     - **Catch what falls through:** "you told Dan 'this week,' it's Thursday, no note it went out ŌĆö did it?" ┬Ę "Adam's quiet on the macro 9d, usually 3 ŌĆö chase?" ┬Ę reading a summary: "new name Sarah at LKQ, not in contacts, sounds like a decision-maker ŌĆö add her?"
     - **Read between the lines of his own notes:** "last two All Star notes read tenser ('still waiting,' 'frustrated') ŌĆö flag cooling?" ┬Ę "the way you described LKQ, sounds like expansion talk ŌĆö bump tier/cadence?"
     - **Produce the artifact, not just the reminder:** "here's a chase email to LKQ's POC + an internal product nudge, both drafted off what you fed me." ┬Ę "Monday pack ready: promised-vs-done, what moved, what's stuck + why." ┬Ę "turn this week's LKQ notes into a team-sheet row?"
     - **Manage HIM, not just accounts (capacity/triage):** "6 commitments due this week, 3 same day ŌĆö 2 can slip unnoticed, 1 angers a supplier; do them in this order." ┬Ę "4 new commitments in today's summaries ŌĆö heavy day; most time-sensitive is the All Star audit."
     - **Root cause under the symptoms (highest wow, build last):** "LKQ's last 4 asks all point at one need ŌĆö reporting; you've solved them one-off; propose ONE project that fixes the root?"
     - **REACHABILITY MAP:** CLOSEST (bones exist, just need the stream flowing in) = pre-call brief ┬Ę dropped-commitment catch ┬Ę chase-email drafts ┬Ę Monday pack ┬Ę recall-on-demand. MIDDLE (new synthesis on data we hold) = cross-account thread-connect ┬Ę tone/momentum from prose ┬Ę capacity triage. FURTHEST (genuine strategist, earn trust first) = root-cause spotting ┬Ę "product problem not account problem." **Across ALL of it the one rule holds: Pip proposes, Chris approves, speaks ONLY when it genuinely has something ŌĆö the 10-mediocre-observations-a-day version is worse than nothing.**
   - **ROUND-4 REFINEMENTS (June 24 2026 ŌĆö 2nd ClaudeŌåöChatGPT exchange + Chris "I want Pip to be a better version of me, not just follow what I do"; Claude vetted, these are KEEPERS):**
     - **­¤öÆ THE 4-PART INSIGHT GATE (lock this for the whole mastermind layer):** every proactive observation MUST answer all four ŌĆö (1) Evidence (what happened), (2) Why it matters (why Chris should care), (3) Proposed action, (4) Expected outcome. **If Pip can't fill all four ŌåÆ it says NOTHING.** This is the concrete enforcement of precision-over-volume ŌĆö not a vibe, a gate.
     - **QUARANTINE bold reframes OUT of operational surfaces.** The pre-call brief / daily brief / waiting board stay GROUNDED + reliable; strategic reframes live in their OWN surface ("Pip's Observations" ŌĆö = the item-52 "connected some dots" card, max 1-2, not necessarily daily). **The line: FACTS flow everywhere (waiting-ons, themes-as-data into account context); OPINIONS/reframes stay quarantined** so a wrong strategic take never poisons the brief Chris depends on daily.
     - **OPPORTUNITY-COST prioritization** ("if you do ONE thing today, do this ŌĆö it touches 3 projects + a relationship at risk"). Underweighted vs pattern-detection; best AMs out-prioritize, not out-remember. CAVEAT: rank on CONCRETE signals (deadline, # stakeholders affected, stall age) ŌĆö never Pip's gut, or a confidently-wrong "do this first" beats a plain list.
     - **­¤öÆ FEATURE-SELECTION TEST (lock it):** "Does this make Pip more ACCURATE about reality, or more USEFUL at changing Chris's decisions? If neither ŌåÆ it's noise disguised as intelligence." The filter that prevents building a very intelligent OBSERVER (trivia) instead of a chief of staff (changes decisions).
     - **ŌŁÉ DECISION JOURNAL ŌĆö the real mechanism for "me, but better" (the best new idea; build LATE = Level 3, after the foundation).** Quietly log the CALLS Chris makes (promoted X to a project ┬Ę escalated Y ┬Ę bumped Z's cadence) + the why + the outcome, so later Pip can say *"last few times something recurred like this you made it a project and it moved ŌĆö do that here?"* Why it's the ONLY true answer to "better than me": a generic "better" (imported best-practice) IS the wtf Chris wants to avoid; "better" only works grounded in HIS OWN track record. Build rules: **INFER decisions from the action he already took (don't interrogate / no forms); HUMBLE on outcomes (correlation, not "works 80%" ŌĆö same no-fabricated-confidence rule); LATE (assumes the grounded layer works).** Likely its own queue item when it's time. The LADDER: L1 remember for me ŌåÆ L2 think like me ŌåÆ L3 improve me; earn each before the next (and note: item 55 proves L1 is currently leaking, so foundation-first).
   - **WHAT WE ALREADY HAVE to build on (don't reinvent):** `useRecentThemes` (cross-account theme detection, already feeds the daily brief), the `waiting_on`/aged-board layer, semantic recall (F6) + `search_notes`, the operator-pass pattern (this is the operator pass pointed at the capture STREAM instead of account-by-account), drip/follow-up questions (the proactive-nudge surface already exists). Mostly a NEW synthesis prompt + a recurrence query over existing rows + a suggestions surface ŌĆö not a new data store (App Coherence: the tasks/captures already ARE the stream; don't add a parallel "stream" table).
   - **THE TWO THINGS THAT MAKE OR BREAK IT (my flags as the honest coworker):** (1) **PRECISION OVER VOLUME or it dies.** Chris's #1 Pip allergy is task/suggestion explosion. A mastermind that suggests a project every time something repeats twice = noise = trust death. HARD threshold + real confidence + "no suggestion is a valid output"; recurrence ŌēĀ importance (something said 3├Ś may just be him thinking out loud ŌĆö Pip must tell "recurring because stuck/important" from "recurring because chatty"). Start with ONE suggestion/day max, earn the right to more. (2) **DATA LINE pressure goes UP with the fire hose.** "Account numbers for X shops" is literally shop identifiers + counts = on the data line. The retained signals + any synthesis output must GENERALIZE ("supplier sending shop account data" not the numbers/list). More raw corporate text flowing in = more chances for numbers to lodge in Pip-authored memory ŌĆö the generalization guards must be tight on the capture-parse AND the synthesis pass.
   - **HOW IT STAYS CHEAP + non-stale (the architecture answer to "see it all"):** NOT a giant always-on context (rejected in item 51). A focused periodic synthesis query over a bounded recent window (last ~7ŌĆō14d of stream items, titles/themes only), one Sonnet call, cached + fingerprint-gated like the operator pass + Monday pack ŌĆö re-runs only when the stream actually moved. Suggestions persist until acted on/dismissed.
   - **OPEN DESIGN Qs for Chris:** where the suggestions surface (Home "Pip connected some dots Ō£”" card? a dedicated synthesis view? inside the daily brief?); cadence (daily, or live as he dumps?); how aggressive (1/day vs. surface-everything-confident); does a promoted suggestion create a Gauge project directly or a draft for him to flesh out. **Depends on item 51's (1b) capture inbox + recurring-theme groundwork ŌĆö build that first, then this is the capstone.**
   - **RESOLVED DESIGN ŌĆö account pin on the dump box (June 24 2026):** the capture inbox gets an OPTIONAL top-level "pin this dump to [account]" dropdown that acts as a **default, NOT a lock**. (a) Single-account brain-dump: pin it ŌåÆ every extracted row with no account of its own lands there (no repeating the name). (b) Email summary across many accounts: leave it blank ŌåÆ Pip routes each row per-line as today. **Rule: per-row account detection ALWAYS overrides the pin** (a line that names its own account wins), so a stray pin can't hijack a multi-account paste. The per-row editable AccountPicker in the review step (already in `QuickCaptureModal`) is the safety net regardless ŌĆö nothing files until confirmed. DO NOT make the pin force ALL rows to one account (that would wreck a multi-account paste). Rule of thumb for Chris: one account on his mind ŌåÆ pin; pasting the daily summary ŌåÆ leave blank.

**53. Desktop autocorrect ŌĆö iPhone-style auto-replace in prose fields (QUEUED June 24 2026, Chris "side thing")** ŌĆö *(NOT built. Chris wants obvious typos + contractions fixed as he types ŌĆö "arent" ŌåÆ "aren't", "teh" ŌåÆ "the" ŌĆö like an iPhone keyboard.)* KEY FACT: on his iPhone the OS keyboard ALREADY autocorrects any text field; the gap is **desktop** (browsers give the red squiggly `spellcheck` underline but do NOT auto-replace). He's 90% desktop, so the payoff is a built-in layer. **Recommended approach (the sweet spot ŌĆö NOT a full dictionary):** a curated high-confidence replacement map ŌĆö contractions (arent/dont/wont/cant/im/ive/youre/theyre/didnt/doesnt/isnt/wasnt/werent/hasnt/havent/wouldnt/couldnt/shouldntŌĆ”) + the few-hundred most-common English typos (tehŌåÆthe, recieveŌåÆreceive, seperateŌåÆseparate, definatelyŌåÆdefinitelyŌĆ”). Fire ONLY on a completed word (space/enter/punctuation), replace in place, leave a one-step undo (Ctrl+Z already works on a textarea edit; optionally backspace-reverts like iOS). **THE ONE GOTCHA that makes or breaks it ŌĆö protect proper nouns / jargon / account names.** Must NOT "correct" Fuse5, MSO, LKQ, account/contact names, or anything capitalized mid-typing ŌĆö those are exactly the words a dumb autocorrect mangles. So: skip capitalized words, skip anything matching the glossary (`folio_pip_facts`) or an account/contact name, keep the map curated (no fuzzy full-dictionary matching ŌåÆ no false positives on names). **Scope:** the big free-text PROSE surfaces only ŌĆö meeting notes editor, quick-capture, note textareas ŌĆö NOT every input (never autocorrect an email/account-name/due-date field). **Coherence:** lives as ONE shared helper (`src/lib/autocorrect.js`) and plugs into the SAME textareas as `useAutoBullet` (which already does sentence auto-capitalization) ŌĆö don't reimplement per surface. **Data-line nuance:** this is a TYPING AID happening visibly as he types (like the keyboard), with undo ŌĆö NOT Pip silently editing saved notes, so it doesn't violate "Pip never silently edits user text" (different thing: a keyboard feature, reversible, user sees it). Deterministic, zero AI cost. **Effort S.** Quick partial win to check first: confirm no prose textarea sets `autoCorrect="off"`/`spellCheck={false}` (that would suppress even the iOS keyboard's native autocorrect on mobile).

**54. Pip learns your HABITS ŌåÆ offers to codify them (QUEUED June 24 2026, Chris ŌĆö the second axis of "wow")** ŌĆö *(NOT built. Chris: "does he have the ability to do things like 'I've noticed you always assign Adam for X task. Want me to hard-code him as the owner of this type of task?'" A DIFFERENT axis from item 52: 52 = patterns in the WORK/RELATIONSHIPS (Tara/projects); THIS = patterns in HOW CHRIS OPERATES (his own workflow habits) ŌåÆ offer to automate them. Both are "wow," complementary.)* The category: **operational pattern learning ŌåÆ proposed defaults/automations.** Pip watches how Chris repeatedly does things and OFFERS to codify each as a reversible default. Examples: "you've assigned Adam the last 4 integration tasks ŌĆö make him the default owner for those?" ┬Ę "you always set audits ~2 weeks out ŌĆö pre-fill that due date?" ┬Ę "every LKQ meeting you create a follow-up ŌĆö auto-suggest it next time?" ┬Ę "you keep re-tagging these as commitments ŌĆö flag this type automatically?"
   - **ŌÜĪ HALF-BUILT ALREADY ŌĆö `pip_assignment_hints` is the engine for the Adam example.** Pip ALREADY learns assignee patterns: `pip_assignment_hints (account_id, task_pattern, assignee_email)` is written when Chris overrides an assignee in the summarize preview, fed back into the next summarize, AND promoted to a cross-account hint (`account_id=null`) once Ōēź3 distinct account-specific hints share the same `task_pattern`+`assignee`. **The gap is it's SILENT** ŌĆö it learns + auto-applies without ever surfacing "I noticed this, want to lock it in?" or showing a receipt when a learned default fires. This item = give that silent learning a VISIBLE, CONSENT-BASED voice (+ extend the same pattern-detectŌåÆoffer shape to due-dates, follow-ups, commitment-tagging, routing).
   - **THE MAGIC DETAIL = RECEIPTS.** When a learned default fires, Pip shows its work: "I set Adam as owner here ŌĆö you usually do. (undo)". That visible feedback is the "Pip is alive / it's learning me" moment Chris has wanted for a while (the receipts theme) AND doubles as proof the capture habit is paying off.
   - **THE TWO RULES (same as everything ŌĆö break them and it's annoyance, not wow):** (1) **PROPOSE, never silently impose** ŌĆö always offers ("want me to lock this in?"), Chris taps yes, everything codified is REVERSIBLE; he's never surprised by Pip having changed how things work. (NB: the current `pip_assignment_hints` auto-applies silently ŌĆö this item should add the offer + receipt so it stops being a black box.) (2) **HIGH BAR** ŌĆö only offer after a REAL pattern (~4 consistent instances), never after 2; recurrence ŌēĀ a rule. A stream of "want me to automate this?" prompts is task-explosion in a nicer hat ŌĆö one good offer beats ten eager ones; "no offer" is the default state.
   - **DATA LINE:** assignee/due-date/routing/tagging patterns are workflow metadata, not business numbers ŌĆö safe. (Don't let a learned "default" ever encode a customer count / shop list / number.)
   - **WHY IT MATTERS:** the difference between an assistant that REMEMBERS and one that ANTICIPATES ŌĆö "I know how you'd do this, want me to just do it?" That's the chief-of-staff feeling, and the assignee half already has its engine. **Surface it where the work happens** (summarize preview, task create, the proposed-default offer as a drip-style card) ŌĆö reuse the existing offer/receipt surfaces, don't add a parallel one (App Coherence). **Build relationship to 52:** these are the two faces of "Pip's proactive intelligence" ŌĆö 52 reasons over content, 54 reasons over Chris's behavior; ship 52's grounded foundation first (north star), then 54 rides the same propose-and-approve plumbing.

**44. Pip 3D redesign ŌĆö "Bold Hex" (DESIGN LOCKED by Chris, June 10 2026 ŌĆö do not alter without his explicit say-so)** ŌĆö Chris approved the **Bold Hex** variant from the v4 mockup (`mockups/pip-hex-ring-final.html`, branch `claude/magical-bohr-ex126v` ŌĆö that file is visual ground truth). The design: Pip's two spheres (current proportions, head bright / tail 0.42) re-skinned as **hex-tiled lattices over a soft glowing core**, floating inside a **hex-tiled torus ring** with an organic drifting twist (not a perfect circle ŌĆö "no tire"), diagonally tilted, visibly spinning. **ONE breath clock (4.8s ŌĆö slowed from 2.4 on June 10 2026, the breath was the perceived-speed problem; classic small orbs keep the 2.4s CSS breathe) drives every hexagon in the figure** ŌĆö ring cells + sphere cells open/close together (`bs = 0.55+0.56┬Ębreath`), ring swells, core glow brightens, all in sync.
   - **FROZEN PARAMETERS** (from the mockup's Bold Hex cfg; changing ANY of these = changing Pip = requires Chris): ring `R 84, rt 18, nu 16, nv 4, tiltX 0.40, tiltY ŌłÆ0.48, spin 0.18 rad/s (slowed from 0.45 by Chris, June 10 2026 ŌĆö too fast at full size), sw 1.6, warp 16, wob 6, fill:false, motionScale 1.0 (knob scales ALL rotation+twist time, never breath; tried 0.4 then reverted ŌĆö the fast motion was the breath)`; ring swell `R├Ś(0.97+0.05┬Ębreath)`, tube `rt├Ś(0.92+0.12┬Ębreath)`; radius waver `1+0.055┬Ęsin(2uŌłÆ0.33t)`, twist `warp┬Ęsin(2u+0.9ŌłÆ0.41t)+wob┬Ęsin(3u+0.27t)`; spheres head `r16 @ (0,ŌłÆ16), n=18 hexes, spin 0.3`, tail `r11.2 @ (0,18), n=10, spin ŌłÆ0.26, opacity 0.42`; hex size `1.9/ŌłÜn`; perspective `FP 480 / FS 5`; 4 depth buckets at z ┬▒0.4 with opacities `.16/.34/.66/.95` and stroke widths `├Ś0.8/0.9/1.05/1.25`; sphere-group breathe `scale 1+0.08┬Ębreath`; colors ONLY from accent tokens (accent / hi / deep) so Life-mode dusty-orange reskins automatically.
   - **Lock-down plan (the "Pip never drifts again" guarantee), to build on ship:** (1) single canonical `PipOrb3D` component, spec as a frozen `PIP_SPEC` constant block ŌĆö every surface renders through it, nothing redraws Pip inline; (2) **deterministic geometry unit test** ŌĆö render one frame at fixed t, assert exact path output; any parameter nudge fails CI (`npm run test` already runs on every push); (3) sizes below ~32px (`xs`/`sm` rail marks) KEEP the current simple two-circle orb ŌĆö hexes mush at tiny sizes; 3D form takes over `lg`+; (4) reduced-motion renders a static frame; (5) on ship, promote this item to a locked "Pip Visual Spec Rule" near the top of CLAUDE.md in the same commit.
   - Status: **Ō£ģ SHIPPED to `main` June 10 2026 PM** ŌĆö built by Sonnet Patch from the frozen spec, reviewed line-by-line by the main session (3 review fixes: live `stateRef` so state changes reach the rAF loop, speaking pulse on the spec'd 0.42s clock, `.pip.pip3d > svg { animation:none }` so classic CSS breathe never fights the JS frames). `PipOrb` routes `lg/xl/xxl` ŌåÆ `PipOrb3D`; `xs/sm/md` keep the classic orb. Drift lock live: 35 tests in `pip3dGeometry.test.js` incl. output hashes. `--accent-hi` token added to all four palettes. Verified rendering live in the real app via headless browser before ship. **Same-day approved tweaks (Chris, in his words):** ring spin 0.45ŌåÆ0.18 (nausea), Home hero orb always `xxl` + `.pip.xxl` 132ŌåÆ160px, and state-tint fix ŌĆö `.pip.thinking`/`.pip.alert` now also override `--accent-hi`/`--accent-deep` (via color-mix) so the 3D form retints as ONE color instead of mixed red/teal. **Round 2 same day:** `motionScale 0.4` (see frozen list) + pulse rings (sonar/heartbeat ::before/::after) suppressed on `.pip3d` ŌĆö the hex ring IS the ring; classic small orbs keep them. **Round 3 same day (final):** breath 2.4ŌåÆ4.8s + motionScale back to 1.0 ŌĆö Chris identified the breath, not the rotation, as the nauseating motion; spin stays 0.18.

Candidates, in priority order:
   - **Tier 1 (signature moments):** `PipLoader` auth/loading screen ŌåÆ small hex torus ring spinner (first screen every morning); Pip **thinking indicators** (chat typing dots + `SummarizeStreamingOverlay`) ŌåÆ 3ŌĆō4 tiny hexes opening/closing on the breath clock; **`PipCard` header strip** ŌåÆ faint hex-edge accent so every Pip-authored card carries the signature; **empty states** ŌåÆ ultra-faint hex lattice watermark (~2ŌĆō3% opacity) behind the copy.

   - **HEX GRAMMAR v1 ŌĆö the structured format (June 11 2026, per Chris: "I want these subtle details throughout the app, all different tabsŌĆ” accounts cards get a touch of it and project cards and task and cadence cards also get the same thing since all of them currently have the same structure"; mockup section "One grammar, every card" in `public/mockups/hex-spread.html`):** four primitives from one helper (`src/lib/hexMotif.jsx` or similar, built on the frozen hex geometry):
     1. **`hexSignature(n, peak)`** ŌĆö fading corner chain (each cell ├Ś0.58 the previous), bottom-right of cards, NEVER animated. **Cell count encodes authorship:** **5 cells @ ~0.30 peak = Pip-authored** (PipCard, operator panel, prepped blocks); **3 cells @ ~0.13 peak = user content** (account cards, Gauge project cards, cadence cards, kanban task cards ŌĆö one identical treatment across the shared card anatomy). Status colors stay on the left edge as today; hexes are ALWAYS accent-colored ŌĆö two channels, never mixed.
     2. **`hexLattice`** ŌĆö uniform watermark ~0.045, empty states only, static.
     3. **`hexField`** ŌĆö radial-falloff lattice (peak ~0.16 fading to 0), Home hero behind the orb + auth screen, static.
     4. **`hexPulse`** ŌĆö breathing cells on the 4.8s clock; ONLY where Pip actively works: loader (ring) + thinking indicators (3 staggered cells).
     **Placement rules:** cards get the signature, **rows NEVER do** ŌĆö a panel of dense rows gets ONE chain on the panel (50 rows, one chain); where a Mark glyph already provides identity (view headers, nav), no hex motif (one identity per surface); opacities are dark-theme values ŌĆö re-tune for light theme at build and verify both (Theme Rule).

   **EXECUTION PROTOCOL (read before building any batch):**
   1. One batch = one Sonnet Patch run in a worktree, phrased per the Patch gotchas ("YOU are Patch ŌĆö EXECUTE NOW; don't end turn until git commit succeeds"). Main session reviews line-by-line, ticks boxes in the SAME commit, ships on Chris's "push."
   2. DB changes apply to prod via MCP migration + fold into `schema.sql` in the same batch.
   3. After ALL batches: run a final verification sweep ŌĆö one agent re-checks every ticked box against the code (the "audit-the-fix" pass). Untickable boxes get re-opened, never deleted.
   4. Sanity-Pass Rule applies to every fix (esp. the silent-failure surfaces: RLS, prompts, cron, localStorage).

   - **THE FIX SET (scoped, low-risk):** ~~(1) correct the 4 cost constants~~ DONE prior session. ~~(2) Wire spend cap into operator-run~~ DONE June 16. (3)ŌĆō(6) above are the remaining levers.
   - **STRATEGY (the Opus answer to "more cost-effective without compromising Pip's intelligence," June 12 2026):** the durable levers, captured so they don't die in chat ŌĆö **(1) Prompt-cache discipline:** the static block (`PIP_PERSONA`+formatting+fewshots) must stay byte-stable; every persona edit (e.g. the item-46 anti-sycophancy line) busts the cache and re-bills full input. Audit which surfaces actually hit cache (chat does ~3.4k cache-read; `pip-state-refresh` + `pip` Haiku show **0 cache** ŌĆö they pay full input every call). **(2) Right-size context per surface, don't dump everything:** intelligence comes from the RIGHT context, not MORE ŌĆö trim per-account context to what the surface needs (the parity rule says wire a field to both paths, NOT that every field goes to every surface). **(3) Tier by reasoning need, not by habit:** Sonnet only where semantic judgment matters (summarize project-matching, chat, daily brief synthesis); Haiku for extraction/compression/classification (already mostly done in Batch 1). **(4) Event-driven over timer-driven:** recompute state on real signals (new meeting, task close, correction logged), never on a clock ŌĆö kills the `pip-state-refresh` waste class and is the operator-run signal-gating principle generalized. **(5) Cache/dedupe expensive once-a-day outputs** (brief, operator report) ŌĆö already saved to DB; never regenerate for the same inputs. **(6) Make spend VISIBLE + capped** (the fixed tile + a real per-day cap that gates the biggest spender) so cost can't silently run away again. Full reasoning in the June 12 chat; this is the durable checklist.
   - **SONNETŌåÆHAIKU AUDIT (June 12 2026 ŌĆö answer to "anywhere I use Sonnet I could use Haiku?"):** 7 Sonnet surfaces exist (`operator-run`, summarize, chat, daily brief, `profile-synthesis`, QBR, `generate-questions`). Verdict: **KEEP Sonnet** on operator-run / summarize / chat / daily brief (real judgment ŌĆö you'd feel the downgrade) and on profile-synthesis + QBR (too rare to save anything, high-stakes output). **Only `generate-questions` is a clean Haiku candidate** (background drip, lowest stakes, already auto-degrades to Haiku over the spend cap). The obvious extraction/transform jobs are ALREADY Haiku (Batch 1 reroutes + per-account brief/email/terminology/state-refresh/leadership-readout). KEY: every Sonnet surface reads a per-surface env override (`PIP_QUESTIONS_MODEL`/`PIP_QBR_MODEL`/`PIP_CHAT_MODEL`/`PIP_OPERATOR_MODEL`/`PIP_DAILY_BRIEF_MODEL`/`PIP_PROFILE_MODEL`), so tier is **A/B-testable in Vercel env with NO deploy** ŌĆö flip `PIP_QUESTIONS_MODEL=claude-haiku-4-5-20251001`, live with it a week, keep it if quality holds. Tiering is NOT where the real money is (the easy moves are done) ŌĆö volume/caching/gating are.
   - **OPERATOR-RUN COST-REDUCTION PASS (June 12 2026 ŌĆö Chris kept it on Sonnet, wants usage down without dumbing it down). MEASURE FIRST against the first night of logs, then cut.** Cost = (deep passes ├Ś per-pass tokens) + 1 roll-up. Levers, ranked, all Sonnet-quality-preserving: **Tier 1 (Ōēłzero quality cost):** (1) **Draft follow-up emails on-demand, not draft-ahead** ŌĆö the email is the biggest *output* chunk (output = 5├Ś input price) and most pre-drafts are never sent; defer to when Chris clicks "draft" (same Sonnet, fresher context). DECIDING QUESTION: does he actually send the pre-drafts? If rarely ŌåÆ free win. (2) **Conditional output fields** ŌĆö emit `agenda` only when a meeting's upcoming, `delta` only when prior state exists (email already conditional). (3) **Skip the roll-up on a genuinely quiet night** ŌĆö carry yesterday's report forward + one-line "nothing new" instead of a fresh Sonnet call. (4) **Right-size per-account context** ŌĆö the uncacheable bulk; trim renderAccountContext to decision-relevant fields (last 1-2 meetings + tone, overdue/commitment tasks, champions/blockers, in-flight projects) ŌĆö careful not to cut signal. **Tier 2 (small tradeoff, bigger savings):** (5) **Delta-update instead of full re-read** ŌĆö feed prior state + "what changed since" and ask to UPDATE, not rebuild; far less in/out for barely-moved accounts (also a continuity *gain*). (6) **Deep sweep 2-3├Ś/week + heuristic-light (no-LLM) the other nights.** **Rejected:** batching many accounts per call (attention dilution + output-limit); longer cache TTL (can't span 24h). Caching the shared user-context (operating_context/profile/glossary, ~3k tok) into the cached system block across the 8 passes ŌĆö separate already-agreed win (currently re-billed 8├Ś in the user message at gatherAndRun ~line 519). Build Tier 1 first; delta-updates as follow-up.

**36. Pip follow-up questions (conversational Teach Pip)** ŌĆö *(Ō£ģ SHIPPED June 16 2026)* When the user answers one of Pip's questions (drip / "Teach Pip" / Catch Up), Pip fires a follow-up that digs into that specific answer ~60% of the time, making Teach Pip feel like a real conversation rather than a form.
   - **Built:** new `api/followup-question.js` Haiku endpoint (JWT auth, `logPipUsage` wired, Anthropic client inside try-catch, `maxDuration:30`). Gates: answer must be Ōēź30 chars, no chaining (follow-up on a follow-up blocked by `source === "followup"` check), terminology questions never get follow-ups. Inserts: `source:'followup'`, `priority:10`, `category:'biographical'`, `trigger_context: "follow-up to question " + questionId`. `PIP_FOLLOWUP_MODEL` env override available.
   - **`usePipDripQuestions.js`:** inner `fetch` callback renamed ŌåÆ `loadRows` throughout (critical: frees the global `fetch` name for use inside `triggerFollowup`). Queue and throttle queries updated to `.in("source", ["gap_observed", "followup"])` so follow-ups surface in the drip queue. `triggerFollowup(question, answerText)` is fire-and-forget (gets session token, calls `/api/followup-question`, calls `loadRows()` on success to surface immediately). `answerAndCount` calls it with `Math.random() < 0.6` gate after every answered question.
   - **Cost guard:** Ōēż1 Haiku call per answer; follow-up rows count toward daily cap (part of `["gap_observed","followup"]` window) but NOT toward the `QUEUE_SOFT_CAP` in `generate-questions` (which still only counts `gap_observed` ŌĆö follow-ups don't block gap detection).

**39. Pip speed ŌĆö stream the meeting summary as it writes** ŌĆö *(Ō£ģ SHIPPED June 10 2026 PM inside Game Plan Phase 1.1d ŌĆö two-phase output: prose recap streams live into SummarizeStreamingOverlay, ===PLAN=== delimiter, JSON plan parses on completion; server already streamed any mode so api/pip.js untouched.)* The slowest user-facing Pip surface is meeting **summarize** (`mode:"summary"`, Sonnet, `max_tokens:3072`, **buffered** ŌĆö you hit "End & Summarize" and stare at a spinner until the whole structured plan is generated). Keep Sonnet quality (don't downgrade to Haiku; don't hard-cap length).

So this is a real change to the summarize flow, not a flag flip. Likely shape: a **two-phase** flow ŌĆö stream a readable prose recap first (visible immediately), then resolve the structured plan and open the preview modal ŌĆö OR restructure the model output so the prose recap comes first as plain text and the JSON plan follows a delimiter, streaming the prose portion live and parsing the plan on completion. **42. Work mode byte-for-byte unchanged. **Fast-follows (not yet done):** NL "tell Pip" capture (structured quick-add only today), LifeŌåÆdaily-brief fusion (unified day), VIP-ladder ŌåÆ real reminder banners/push, Life bottom nav is single-Home for now.
   - **PHASE 2 (NEXT, the headline feature) ŌĆö the honey-do BRAIN:** Pip as a home-project partner ŌĆö how-to coaching, materials/tools to buy, step-by-step, troubleshooting mid-project, complexity reasoning. Deep-dive with Chris before building. (Honey-do today only remembers + prioritizes.)
   - **Mode system:** a `data-mode="work"|"life"` attribute on `<html>` (parallel to `data-theme`), persisted to `localStorage` (`folio_mode`), via a `useMode()` hook modeled on `useTheme()`. Default work. Pre-mount inline script in `index.html` sets it (no flash), same as theme.
   - **Theme (dusty blue):** Life mode reskins via `[data-mode="life"]` CSS-var overrides in `index.html` ŌĆö accent + shades swap from work green to **dusty blue (lightŌåÆdark shades, mirroring how work is shades of green)**. Reuses the token architecture (every `C.*` is a `var(--ŌĆ”)`), so the whole app recolors instantly with no remount. Must work in BOTH dark and light themes (so `[data-theme][data-mode]` combinations). Green stays canonical for work; blue = off the clock ŌĆö a psychological signal.
   - **Toggle placement (LOCKED):** **desktop** ŌĆö bottom-left by the CV/avatar in the user-menu corner of the rail. **Mobile** ŌĆö the toggle takes the global header spot where **+Account** currently lives; **+Account moves up into the top of the Accounts tab** (it's account-specific anyway).
   - **Life module + Life Home (the 3 cards):** (1) **Upcoming** ŌĆö what's on the calendar soon (appointments + events). One table, `kind` in (`appointment`|`event`|`todo`): common cols `title, notes, date, time, location, status, opened_at, complexity, recurrence` (e.g. annual for events), `importance` tier, `lead_ladder` (or derive from importance). Fold into `schema.sql` + new `supabase/life_items.sql`; apply to prod via MCP.
   - **Important events ŌĆö VIP heads-up ladder (LOCKED: tiers-with-defaults + Pip auto-flags the obvious ones):** events carry an **importance tier**; VIP (anniversary, spouse/kids birthdays, Christmas) get a **multi-stage escalating ladder** ŌĆö ~3wk soft ("start thinking") ŌåÆ 1wk ("got a plan?") ŌåÆ 3d ("order now so it ships in time") ŌåÆ 1d + day-of (hard). Normal events get a short few-day runway. VIP nudges are more insistent (cost of forgetting is high). **Recurs annually** ŌĆö set the date once, Pip carries it forward forever. Pip infers importance from title ("anniversary"/"wife's birthday" obviously high-stakes); user can override. (Phase 2: Pip helps with the gift ŌĆö ideas + order-by dates.)
   - **Capture:** plain-language to Pip ("dentist Tuesday at 3", "honey-do: rebuild the back gate") ŌåÆ filed into the right `kind`. Phase 1 may start with a structured quick-add and layer NL parse as a fast-follow.

Work mode stays 100% unchanged (Life is additive). **Phase 2 = the honey-do BRAIN** (the part Chris most wants): Pip as a home-project partner ŌĆö complexity reasoning, how-to coaching, materials/steps, troubleshooting mid-project. Deep-dive after the structure ships.
   - **Pip parity:** eventually Life items feed the daily brief so the morning read is the WHOLE day (work + life). Phase 1 keeps Life self-contained; brief fusion is the first fast-follow.

<details><summary>original spec</summary>

**Gauge project "Latest update" pulse log** ŌĆö a quick status-update field on each Gauge project, distinct from the existing `notes` blob (notes = durable scratchpad; updates = timestamped running heartbeat). **Design locked:**
    - **Storage:** `status_updates jsonb default '[]'` on `gauge_projects` ŌĆö array of `{ body, at (ISO), by (user email) }`, newest-first. No new table, no join; rides the existing `updateProject` path. The array *is* the history.
    - **Model: append-only.** Each save prepends a new timestamped entry; the previous becomes history. `at` auto-stamped on save; `by` auto-captured (matters for Leader view). Typo fixes happen in the project edit box, not inline.
    - **Expanded card (GaugeView):** one-line "Latest update" field showing the current pulse + muted relative timestamp ("Updated 2h ago ┬Ę Jun 4"). Type + Enter/Save prepends.
    - **Edit box (ProjectModal):** "Status history" read-only list ŌĆö every past update with timestamp + author.
    - **Pip wiring (parity rule ŌĆö both paths):** inject latest + the prior two (for momentum sense) into `pipContext.js` (chat) AND `pip.js` (summarize), plus daily/portfolio brief, leadership readout, and cadence pre-call brief. Lets briefs say "All Star ŌĆö latest: 'waiting on legal sign-off' (Jun 3)." Keep it cheap: latest + last 2 only.
    - SQL: new `supabase/gauge_project_status_updates.sql` + fold into canonical `schema.sql`. Docs: update `docs/product-overview.md` (Gauge capability) + `docs/upgrades.md` entry on ship.

</details>

34. **Pip Autonomous Operator ŌĆö ~~nightly loop~~ MANUAL-TRIGGER loop + materialized operator state + dynamic Pip cards everywhere** ŌĆö *(Phases 1, 2 & 2.5 SHIPPED June 8 2026. **ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ TRIGGER CHANGED June 17 2026: the nightly Vercel cron was RETIRED ŌĆö the operator now runs ONLY when Chris taps "Run Pip's pass" on Home.** Cost decision: it ran every morning whether or not he opened the app, and the report rarely changed his day. `vercel.json` `crons` entry removed; `api/operator-run.js` now also accepts a user JWT (scopes the run to that user) so the browser button can trigger it without the cron secret; `OperatorRunButton` on Home drives it. The engine/output/state below are otherwise unchanged ŌĆö wherever this spec says "cron" / "nightly" / "overnight," read "on manual trigger." See the June 17 2026 handoff.)* turn Pip from a pull-triggered advisor into a scheduled agent that works the book of business and pre-fills every Pip surface in the app. The morning brief is the read-only *head* of this; the loop is the body. **Design locked:**

    - **Phase 1 status (built):** the engine + the Home operator report. Built: `api/operator-run.js` (cron endpoint ŌĆö CRON_SECRET-gated, service-role, runs every morning, signal-gated deep passes capped at 8/run on Sonnet **run in parallel waves of 4** (`maxDuration:60`; sequential calls blew past Vercel's function timeout and killed the run after ~5 accounts before it wrote the report ŌĆö fixed June 8 2026), one portfolio roll-up call, propose-only); **(weekend opt-in gate was built then PULLED June 8 2026 at Chris's request ŌĆö caused testing confusion and saved only pennies; the loop now runs daily, signal-gating alone controls cost);** `vercel.json` cron at `0 9 * * *` (~5am ET); schema (`supabase/pip_operator.sql` ŌĆö operator_* columns on `folio_pip_account_state` + new `folio_operator_reports` table, **applied to prod via MCP + folded into schema.sql**); `src/hooks/useOperatorReport.js`; registered in `scripts/test-api-imports.js`; docs + PDFs. **Deploy state (LIVE):** `CRON_SECRET` is set in Vercel and the cron fires daily (~5am ET); `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` + `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` already set; `OPERATOR_TZ` (default America/New_York) + `PIP_OPERATOR_MODEL` (default claude-sonnet-4-6) left at defaults. Manual run: `GET /api/operator-run?secret=<CRON_SECRET>&user=<uuid>` ŌĆö **a human's `?secret=` query call always runs** (the gone weekend-gate + no skip), the cron uses Bearer auth. **The report is rebuilt each run from the whole prepped book** (this run's fresh deep passes + accounts still carrying recent operator state, last 4 days) so a quiet day still yields a Home report for ~1 roll-up call; it **never clobbers a good same-day report with an empty one** (clobber bug fixed June 8 ŌĆö report keyed `(user, local date)`, only written when there's content). **Operator REPORT output is structured** `{ headline, opening, sections:[{kind:fire|watch|win|signal, items:[{account_name, line, action, has_draft}]}] }`, stored headlineŌåÆ`headline`, openingŌåÆ`report_prose`, sectionsŌåÆ`plan_items` (jsonb). Per-account deep pass (`ACCOUNT_SYSTEM`) returns `{ headline, situation, risks[], draft_email, proposed_moves[], agenda, delta }` ŌåÆ operator_* columns.

    - **Phase 2.5 (built ŌĆö unified Pip card + Home redo, June 8 2026):** shared `src/components/PipCard.jsx` shell ŌĆö one anatomy everywhere: HEAD (Ō£” Pip label + timestamp, a high-level **headline**, a density row of count chips) always visible; BODY collapsed by default ("Show details Ō¢Š"). `OperatorPanel` composes it (head = `operator_headline` + `N risks ┬Ę draft ┬Ę N moves`; body = situation/delta/risks/draft/moves). **Amber unread-notification glow** (`pip-unread` + `pipUnreadPulse` keyframe, `--c-yellow-glow` token both themes): card pulses amber + "NEW" dot when `operator_generated_at` is newer than this device's last-open (localStorage `folio_op_read_<acct>`), clears on expand. New per-account `operator_headline` column (prompt + migration applied to prod + schema.sql + pip_operator.sql). **Home redo ŌåÆ dashboard of cards** (iterated live with Chris over several rounds; final shape): the operator REPORT output is structured (see Phase 1 status). HomeView renders, top-to-bottom: greeting + **centered heartbeat orb** (`.pip.heartbeat`, ~3.4s slowed thump-thump-rest, reduced-motion-gated; `PipOrb heartbeat` prop) ŌåÆ a **"Ō£” Pip" read card** (the Pip-voiced `opening` paragraph + worked/time) ŌåÆ a **full-width, bigger "Today" card** (the `fire` section) ŌåÆ **This week / Pattern / Good news** as separate cards in a **2-up grid** (stacked mobile), content-only (a section with no items doesn't render). Every section row is tappable (account Glow + Open + inline **"Ō£” Draft ready"** that copies the drafted email ŌĆö drafts/commitments fused into rows, no separate cards). The short Pip one-liner under the orb (`pickHeroLine`, rewritten to short/accurate/varied lines from real counts ŌĆö *"Busy one today. Let's dig in."* / *"Slow day ŌĆö good time to warm up a cold account."*) is **dropped whenever an operator report is active** (`operatorActive` flag), since the read card says it better; it only shows on the fallback/no-operator path. Commitment-nudge + live-daily-brief cards suppressed when a report has content. **Pip personality** dialed up in `REPORT_SYSTEM` (dry wit + slightly anxious + loyal, examples + a never-say-filler rule) concentrated in the `headline` + `opening`; section `line`s stay tight. Per-account fallback (no operator state yet) = lightweight heuristic head-only `PipCard` on the account Overview. **Not yet propagated:** the unified PipCard + glow onto Cadence/Gauge (those still use the Phase-2 read-only blocks); Calendar strip; PWA push.

    - **Phase 2 status (built ŌĆö dynamic cards):** the materialized state is read by every relevant surface (no extra LLM call on open; data already loads via `usePipAccountState`'s `select("*")`). Built: shared `src/components/OperatorPanel.jsx` (per-account lens ŌĆö situation, "since last run" delta, risk chips, drafted email Copy/Mail, proposed moves each with **+ Add task / Dismiss**; approve creates a `folio_task` and marks the move `status:applied` in the jsonb so it doesn't reappear; dismiss marks `status:dismissed`) wired into **AccountDetail** (between header and tabs); **CadenceHub** read-only "Pip prepped this overnight" block (situation + suggested agenda) above the cadence brief on account cadences; **GaugeView/PipGaugeCard** "Ō£” Pip proposes" cross-account decision queue (flattens pending `operator_proposed_moves` across `pipAcctState.states`, approve ŌåÆ `insertTask` + mark applied). All guarded to render nothing until `operator_generated_at` exists, so the app is visually unchanged until the loop first runs. **Remaining slivers (NOT built):** Calendar plan-projection strip (deliberately deferred ŌĆö would duplicate Home's report + risks the "don't make it busy" lesson; needs `userId` threaded into the presentational `CalendarView`); optional PWA push companion ("Pip has your operator report Ō£”", content stays in-app).

    - **The loop:** Vercel cron runs nightly, weekday mornings (SunŌåÆThu nights). Sweeps the portfolio via the *existing* Pip endpoints ŌĆö no new permissions, no email/corporate integration (deliberately off the table: compliance + Chris can get in trouble forwarding customer data). For each account that *moved*, runs a deep per-account pass (read account ŌåÆ decide next action ŌåÆ draft the artifact ŌåÆ propose assignee/agenda). Accounts that didn't move ride the cheap compressed path. The loop is **not latency-bound**, so it can afford per-account reasoning the synchronous brief can't (the brief is one compressed Sonnet call because you're staring at a spinner; the loop is unhurried batch depth).

    - **The loop:** Vercel cron runs nightly, weekday mornings (SunŌåÆThu nights). Sweeps the portfolio via the *existing* Pip endpoints ŌĆö no new permissions, no email/corporate integration (deliberately off the table: compliance + Chris can get in trouble forwarding customer data). For each account that *moved*, runs a deep per-account pass (read account ŌåÆ decide next action ŌåÆ draft the artifact ŌåÆ propose assignee/agenda). Accounts that didn't move ride the cheap compressed path. The loop is **not latency-bound**, so it can afford per-account reasoning the synchronous brief can't (the brief is one compressed Sonnet call because you're staring at a spinner; the loop is unhurried batch depth).

    - **Materialized operator state (the core architecture):** the loop writes a per-account "operator state" object to Supabase ŌĆö extends existing `pip_account_state` / `folio_account_snapshots` (decide `pip_account_state` extension vs. new `folio_operator_state` at build). Holds: situation, flagged risks, **pre-drafted follow-up email(s)**, proposed task/project moves, pre-built cadence agenda, and a **"what changed since last run" delta**. This object is the single source of truth.

    - **Dynamic Pip cards = lenses on one brain:** every Pip surface *reads the materialized state* instead of making its own LLM call on open. Same brain, different window per surface:
        - **Home** ŌåÆ the "operator report": prioritized plan with pre-drafted artifacts to approve/adjust/send (evolves the daily brief from "what's happening" ŌåÆ "what's happening + I drafted it").
        - **Cadence Hub** ŌåÆ pre-built agenda + queued drafts for that account, instant (replaces the current on-open Haiku brief call).
        - **Gauge / PipGaugeCard** ŌåÆ proposed project moves as a *decision queue* ("stalled 14d, re-route the legal task to Dana ŌĆö approve?").
        - **Account detail / Brief Me** ŌåÆ brief pre-written + delta since last look.
        - **Calendar** ŌåÆ the plan projected onto the timeline.
        - Side benefit: this **kills the parity-rule drift** ŌĆö one materialized brain means no more hand-wiring each new field into both `pipContext.js` *and* `pip.js`. (Until fully migrated, keep both paths fed.)

    - **Three locked guardrails:**
        1. **Signal-gated** ŌĆö deep passes only on accounts that changed (snapshot/activity diff); the rest stay cheap. If *nothing* moved, there's **no run** ŌĆö work scales to what changed.
        2. ~~**Weekend opt-in**~~ ŌĆö *(designed, built, then PULLED June 8 2026 at Chris's request.)* The loop runs every morning regardless of day; signal-gating (guardrail 1) is the sole cost control. Rationale for the pull: the weekend skip created real testing confusion (a Sunday manual run kept "skipping") for only pennies of weekend savings. If ever wanted back, the logic lived in `processUser` (weekday check + `folio_activity`/`folio_tasks` write-since-last-run count).
        3. **Pre-compute once, render everywhere, refresh only on real signal** ŌĆö cards read pre-computed DB state (a net *cost reduction* on per-surface opens: DB read vs. LLM call). Refresh a card only on a genuine event (new meeting summarized, task closed) ŌĆö **never on a timer, never on every render.** Respects the render-thrash concern + the "don't make it busy" lesson from the revenue rip. Dynamic ŌēĀ constantly recomputing.

    - **Cost model:** one batched Sonnet sweep/morning over *changed accounts only* (Ōēż12 deep passes + 1 roll-up); per-card opens become DB reads. Net per-surface cost goes *down*.

    - **Push layer (optional companion):** PWA push ŌĆö "Pip has your operator report Ō£”" ŌĆö content stays in-app (no account names in the notification text, nothing on a lockscreen). Turns Pip pullŌåÆpush without leaking anything.

    - **Positioning:** the leap from "external brain you feed" ŌåÆ "digital chief of staff that works the book." Defensible angle: **institutional relationship memory that runs itself** ŌĆö the context never walks out the door when an AM leaves.

    - **On ship:** SQL + fold into `schema.sql`; `docs/product-overview.md` (Pip capability) + `docs/upgrades.md` entry + regenerate PDFs. Parity rule applies until the materialized state fully replaces dual-wiring.

- Ō£ģ **Pip question-pipeline RLS fix (June 2026)** ŌĆö "Pip, ask me more" (and the terminology drip) silently produced nothing for weeks. Root cause: `api/generate-questions.js` + `api/detect-terminology.js` built a plain **anon** Supabase client and only used the JWT to *validate* the user ŌĆö they never attached it to the client. Under RLS the anon client read **zero** of the user's accounts (so `generate-questions` bailed with `no_accounts`) and the `folio_pip_questions` insert was **rejected** ŌĆö confirmed against the live DB (anon insert ŌåÆ *"new row violates row-level security policy"*). Fixed by building the client with `global.headers.Authorization = "Bearer " + token` so every read/insert runs as the user. The whole question pipeline (Lane C terminology + Lane D portfolio) was affected. **See the new "Supabase Server-Client Auth Rule" near the top** to prevent recurrence. Found while debugging Chris's live "questions button hasn't been working" report; the stress-bot's `teachpip` scenario now guards it.
- Ō£ģ **"Off the clock" personal soccer card ŌĆö Home (June 2026)** ŌĆö a personal-interest card at the bottom of Home: soccer news (free Guardian RSS, no key) for Man United / Brazil / USMNT / World Cup, plus **live + upcoming scores** via API-Football. `api/sports.js` (server-side so it dodges corporate proxies + keeps the key off the client) fetches RSS + scores, caches in-memory (30 min normally, 120s when a followed team is live), resolves API-Football team ids by name-search (cached), and **degrades to news-only** if the key/API is missing or errors ŌĆö never breaks Home. `useSportsFeed` hook (5-min client cache) + `src/views/home/SportsCard.jsx` (LIVE ŌŚÅ/min, upcoming kickoff, news headlines with topic chips). Hide toggle: Settings ŌåÆ "Off the clock" (localStorage `folio_show_sports`) + a "hide" link on the card itself. **Needs Vercel env `API_FOOTBALL_KEY`** (free tier, 100 req/day) for scores ŌĆö news works without it. Registered in `scripts/test-api-imports.js`. *(Scores built defensively without live testing ŌĆö team-id/free-tier coverage may need a tweak pass once the key's in.)*
- Ō£ģ **Account-merge data-loss fix (June 2026)** ŌĆö `folio_merge_accounts` predated the `folio_items`ŌåÆ`folio_tasks` unification and the account-updates calendar, so merging an account stranded its action items (`folio_tasks`) and update-log rows (`folio_account_updates`) on the now-inactive source ŌĆö silent data loss a daily user would only notice when the data went missing. Added re-parenting for both tables; applied to production via migration `fix_merge_accounts_reparent_tasks_and_updates` (which also synced prod to the canonical integer-returning version), and updated `supabase/schema.sql` + `supabase/inactive_and_merge.sql` to match. **Found by inspecting the live DB while building the stress-bot's merge-integrity test** (which now guards it). Also shipped same session: the `account.name.split` ErrorBoundary crash on Accounts/Partners views, guarded in `AccountDetailHeader.jsx` (`account.name || ""`); and `vite.config.js` `sourcemap:"hidden"` so prod crash stacks decode to real `src/` lines. See the Stress-Bot section for the testing harness those came out of.
- Ō£ģ **Teach Pip ŌĆö on-demand "build his knowledge base" mode (June 2026)** ŌĆö Chris wanted to deliberately sit down and have Pip fire questions to build context, not just wait for the gentle weekly drip. The `PipCatchUp` "Catch up with Pip" surface already answered the whole queue in a sitting, but (a) it was only reachable when a drip question was already showing, and (b) the generator self-throttles (6h + skip when Ōēź5 queued), so it ran dry after ~5. Fixes: (1) **`/api/generate-questions` manual mode** ŌĆö `body { manual:true }` bypasses the backlog cap (`QUEUE_SOFT_CAP`) and asks for a bigger batch (`maxNew` 5ŌåÆ8). (2) **App `teachPipMore()`** ŌĆö calls the manual endpoint bypassing the 6h localStorage throttle, then `dripHook.refetch()` to pull the new questions in. (3) **PipCatchUp "Pip, ask me more ŌåÆ"** ŌĆö a persistent footer button (and an empty-state CTA) that runs `teachPipMore` so the session keeps going as long as you like; `onAskMore` prop. (4) **Persistent entry points** ŌĆö a "Teach Pip about your world" card on Home when no question is queued, and a "Catch up with Pip ŌåÆ" button in Settings ŌåÆ Pip's Questions (both open the global `catchUpOpen`). Everything still flows into `profile_prose` + `folio_pip_facts`, so it compounds into better briefs. No schema changes. **Two follow-up fixes (same day):** (a) the Home "Teach Pip" card's `PipOrb` used `size={18}` (a number) ŌĆö but `PipOrb`'s `size` is a string enum (`"xs"`ŌĆ”`"xxl"`), so it fell back to the giant centerpiece orb and crushed the card text into a one-word-per-line column on mobile; fixed to `size="sm" isStatic`. (b) **"Pip, ask me more" returned nothing** when the queue was empty: the endpoint runs fine (reads work ŌĆö it generated 6 on Jun 5), but **Sonnet returns an empty array** once a thorough set is answered ("return empty if nothing insightful" + full already-asked list). Fixed two ways: a manual-mode prompt override telling Pip the user explicitly wants more (don't abstain, dig per-account), AND a **deterministic account-anchored fallback** ŌĆö if a manual run still yields 0 from the model, generate concrete grounded questions ("Where do things stand with <Account> ŌĆö what are you trying to move, who decides, what could derail it?", accounts with no objective first, skipping internal teams + already-asked) so manual "ask me more" can never dead-end. Endpoint now returns `{ inserted, modelReturned }` for observability.

- Ō£ģ **12-item audit bug batch (June 2026)** ŌĆö Fixed in one commit across 15 files: (1) stuck project detection used `s.done/s.done_at` but stages use `s.completed_at` ŌĆö every in-progress project was falsely flagged stuck; (2) `update_account_health` Pip tool wrote to dead `status` column instead of `status_override` ŌĆö voice/chat health commands were silently no-ops; (3) `leadership-readout.js` filtered on `"green"/"yellow"/"red"` but snapshots store `"healthy"/"watching"/"at_risk"` ŌĆö boss readout always showed zero counts; (4) `allItems` in App.jsx loaded once with no realtime sync ŌĆö Home and Commitments lagged until page reload; (5) `detectKnowledgeGaps` gated on `onboarding_status === "done"` but `profile-synthesis.js` never returned that value ŌĆö Phase-2 question drip was permanently dormant; (6) `business-review.js` had no rate limit; (7) 1:1 portfolio brief lacked `overdue_items` array ŌĆö couldn't name specific overdue items; (8) `pipIntent.js` routed "summarize"/"email" phrases into persona-stripped JSON modes without account context ŌĆö broken chat replies; (9) `useToneTrend.js` NEGATIVE list contained words that never appear in stored `pip_tone` values ŌĆö "Cooling Ōåś" pill never fired correctly; (10) contact assignee in `PipSummarizePreview` used `c.name` as value, landing names in the `assignee_email` column; (11) `callPortfolioBriefPip` and `callBusinessReviewPip` in `pip.js` were missing auth headers ŌĆö daily brief and QBR silently 401'd on every call; (12) `closeItem` and `useCommitmentNudges.markDone` set only one of `done`/`status` ŌĆö split-brain between commitment nudge system and item lists.
- Ō£ģ **Gauge project auto-complete (June 2026)** ŌĆö `ProjectStageEditor.commitStages()` now checks if all stages have `completed_at` set after every toggle. - Ō£ģ **Pip daily brief overhaul ŌĆö 11 items (June 2026)** ŌĆö Root cause: brief was account-health-centric only; if all 37 accounts computed "healthy," Pip said "quiet morning" even when the AM had overdue tasks, commitments due, and stuck projects. Full fix in three batches:
  - **Workload data** ŌĆö brief now receives overdue tasks (by name), overdue commitments, commitments due this week, today's cadences, stuck projects (named + account), cold healthy accounts (30+ days no contact), unsummarized draft meetings, account objective for flagged accounts

  - **Prompt rewrite** ŌĆö explicit triage order (overdue commitments ŌåÆ fires ŌåÆ Major overdue ŌåÆ stuck/cadences ŌåÆ cold), length-scaling rule (2-3 sentences clean / 5-7 heavy), one-paragraph-break structure rule, "end urgent items with a concrete next action" rule
  - **Callout schema upgrade** ŌĆö callouts now include `action` (verb phrase), `priority` (now/this_week/watch), `tier`; HomeView chips render priority-colored dot, bold action verb, `[M]` tier badge
  - **Health momentum delta** ŌĆö `useAccountSnapshots` now fetches 8 days of history; brief computes accounts trending worse (healthyŌåÆwatchingŌåÆat_risk) or recovering, surfaces them with directional label
  - **Tone trend** ŌĆö accounts with 2+ negative/mixed `pip_tone` readings in last 3 days flagged as "COOLING"; warming trend surfaced too
  - **Champions + blockers** ŌĆö `allContacts` threaded from App.jsx into HomeView; brief includes champion and blocker names per account so Pip can factor relationship power map into next-step recommendations
  - **Cross-account themes** ŌĆö `useRecentThemes` (already existed, was unused) now wired to brief; themes appearing on 3+ accounts flagged as portfolio signals (e.g. "pricing came up on 4 accounts this month")
  - Cache key bumped to `v6` on final batch so brief regenerates immediately

- Ō£ģ **Cadence meeting reminders (Pip pre-call nudges)** ŌĆö `useCadenceReminders` hook ticks every 30s, computes each cadence's next occurrence via `getNextOccurrence` + `meeting_time`, fires three thresholds (30m / 5m / start) as in-app `MeetingReminderBanner` rows at the top of the app. Fired + dismissed sets persist in localStorage (`folio_cadence_reminders_fired` / `folio_cadence_reminders_dismissed`) so a refresh never replays. Browser `Notification` API fires system pop-ups when permission granted. One-time discreet "Want Pip to ping you?" prompt surfaces the first time a cadence with a `meeting_time` exists. - Ō£ģ **Smarter Pip summarize + preview modal** ŌĆö `summarizeDraftPip` now receives existing open items + in-flight Gauge tasks + org members + learned assignment hints, and returns a structured `plan[]` (new_item / update_item / close_item / new_task / update_task / skip) instead of a flat action-item list. ## Ripped (deliberate simplification)

Personal Mode focus. Schema stays for future re-build when corporate data integration lands.

- ­¤¬ō **Pipeline V2 + Revenue History + Shop Metrics + revenue surfaces (May 2026)** ŌĆö the Pipeline nav item, `PipelineView`, Log Month modal, MoM/YoY deltas, sparklines on account cards, MoM trend arrows, revenue display in account card meta + account detail header, Revenue YTD + Revenue Trend + Shop Connections cards on Overview, revenue input on AddAccountModal, Shop Metrics overlay, `useAccountMetrics` hook, financial helpers in `metricsUtils.js` (`displayRevenue`, `fmtRevenue`, `momPct`, `yoyPct`, `momDelta`, `fmtPct`, `fmtDelta`, `latestRecord`, `accountRecords`, `MONTH_NAMES`, `parseRevenueText`), `metricsUtils.test.js`, "revenue" sort option, pipeline mark in Onboarding tour, Pipeline filters from the wishlist, "Revenue/tier/pipeline don't apply" notes in Pip context, revenue/shop secondary-signal sentences in `accountInsights.jsx`, `revenueTrend` + `shopConnections` in PipView context payload. DB columns (`revenue`, `revenue_amount`, `folio_revenue_history`, `folio_shop_metrics`) intact. ShopsTab on MSO accounts stayed (operational child shop list). `pickV` survives in `metricsUtils.js` because it's reused across non-financial insight builders. The `pipeline` glyph in `Mark.jsx` stays in the family. Why: Folios is a notepad-on-steroids / external brain ŌĆö revenue surfaces showed empty data and made the app feel busy without delivering value. Compliance blocks real revenue ingestion for the foreseeable future; git history is the safety net.

**Security hardening ŌĆö shipped in code, two items need Supabase dashboard toggle:**

- Ō£ģ Rate limiting on Pip API (20 req/min per user, in-memory)
- Ō£ģ Hardcoded anon key removed ŌĆö env vars only
- Ō£ģ Audit log SQL written (`supabase/audit_log.sql`) ŌĆö run when ready
- Ō£ģ Session timeout ŌĆö 60 min inactivity auto-logout
- Ō£ģ Password strength enforcement ŌĆö 8 chars, uppercase, number required on signup
- ŌÜÖ’ĖÅ **Email verification** ŌĆö enable in Supabase Dashboard ŌåÆ Auth ŌåÆ Settings ŌåÆ "Enable email confirmations"
- ŌÜÖ’ĖÅ **2FA (TOTP)** ŌĆö enable in Supabase Dashboard ŌåÆ Auth ŌåÆ Settings ŌåÆ "Enable MFA"
- ­¤ö£ Active sessions page ŌĆö UI to view/revoke sessions (not yet built)

## Feature Wishlist / Roadmap

High and medium priority items are now in the **Pending Updates** queue above.

### Cadence (once built)
- [ ] **Cadence analytics** ŌĆö meeting frequency per account, open item age, account health trends over time, Pip flags accounts untouched in 30+ days. Hold until enough data exists to make it meaningful.
- [ ] **Power BI integration** ŌĆö connect Supabase directly to Power BI via Postgres connection string for full dashboard reporting. No special integration needed, just expose the DB connection. Hold until data volume justifies it.

### Future / bigger features
- [ ] **Render thrash detector** ŌĆö Phase 6 observability catches React errors and uncaught exceptions, but it doesn't catch infinite render/refetch loops (the app isn't crashing, just spinning). Example bite: the Activity dropdown strobing because `fromDate` recomputed `Date.now()` every render ŌåÆ filters identity changed ŌåÆ useActivity refetched in a loop. The error boundary never fired. Idea: lightweight render-rate detector at the App level ŌĆö if a hook's effect fires > N times in M seconds, log a `error_type='render_thrash'` row to `folio_errors` with the suspicious hook name + stack. Surfaces silent perf disasters before users notice the fans spinning. Not v1.
- [ ] **Unified org vocabulary layer** ŌĆö aliases (item 27), the glossary (`folio_pip_facts`), terminology gap-detection (item 10 Lane C), and account/brand mappings are all the same thing wearing different hats: "what this team calls things." Once each piece is mature, collapse them into one shared org-scoped knowledge base that every Pip surface reads from ŌĆö one place that holds brands, internal codenames, distributor names, program names, person shorthands, and preferred phrasing. This is what makes the whole app feel like it *knows you*. Don't build until the constituent pieces (27, glossary, 10-Lane-C) have shipped and proven their shape; this is the consolidation pass that unifies them.
- [ ] **Lanyard real auth** ŌĆö connect Lanyard users to Folios users via Supabase Auth
- [ ] **Lanyard ŌåÆ Folios live sync** ŌĆö post-conference notes flow into Folios automatically once auth is shared
- [ ] **CRM integrations** ŌĆö Salesforce / HubSpot sync
- [ ] **Mobile app** ŌĆö React Native wrapper or PWA improvements
- [ ] **Revenue-impact Update Calendar v3 ŌĆö Ambitious (supplier webhook / portal / email parser)** ŌĆö deferred follow-up. The v1 build (manual entry + external_event type) shipped ŌĆö see Already shipped: Revenue-impact Update Calendar. v3 would add an auto-ingestion lane so supplier-side and customer-internal changes get logged without manual entry. Big lift; revisit when v1 has enough data to prove the value.
